
1a1(rgyud 'grel): bsdus pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po dus kyi 'khor lo'i 'grel bshad rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi rjes su 'jug pa stong phrag bcu gnyis pa dri ma med pa'i 'od ces bya ba bzhugs/ /
1b1(rgyud 'grel): rgya gar skad du/ bi ma la pra b+hA nA ma mU la tan+t+ra nu sA ri NI dwA da sha sA ha sri ka la g+hu kA la tsakra tan+t+ra rA dza TI kA/
1b2(rgyud 'grel): bod skad du/ bsdus pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po dus kyi 'khor lo'i 'grel bshad rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi rjes su 'jug pa stong phrag bcu
1b3(rgyud 'grel): gnyis pa dri ma med pa'i 'od ces bya ba/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo la phyag 'tshal lo/ /stong nyid snying rje'i bdag nyid can/ /
1b4(rgyud 'grel): srid gsum skye dang 'jigs pa med/ /shes dang shes bya gcig pa'i sku/ /dpal ldan dus 'khor la phyag 'tshal/ /
2a1(rgyud 'grel): rnam par bcas kyang rnam med bcom ldan 'das ma shes rab ma ste de yis 'khyud/ /skye 'jig spangs pa'i 'gyur
2a2(rgyud 'grel): med bde ba dang ldan bzhad pa la sogs bde ba spangs/ /sangs rgyas rnams kyi skye mdzad sku gsum dag dang ldan zhing dus gsum yang
2a3(rgyud 'grel): dag rig /kun mkhyen mchog gi dang po'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan gnyis med de nyid la phyag 'tshal/ /sangs rgyas seng ge'i
2a4(rgyud 'grel): khrir bzhugs rdo rje'i rnal 'byor rnam par dag pa srid pa gsum gyis mchod/ /de nyid gcig pu sku yi rab tu dbye bas rnam pa
2b1(rgyud 'grel): bcu drug srid med srid par gnas/ /shes dang shes bya gcig gyur rgyal ba mchog gi dam tshig yan lag rnam pa bcu gnyis kyi/ /bden don byang
2b2(rgyud 'grel): chub sems ni rgyal po'i rdo rje'i tshig gyur dus kyi 'khor lo la phyag 'tshal/ /kun mkhyen ye shes sku ni rgyal ba'i bdag po'i lhan cig skyes dang de bzhin
2b3(rgyud 'grel): chos kyi sku/ /longs spyod rdzogs dang sprul pa'i sku yang nyin byed sku dang pad+ma'i 'dab ma rgyas pa'i spyan/ /rnam par thar dang sku gsung thugs chags srid
2b4(rgyud 'grel): 'das 'byor pa rnal 'byor dag pa shes rab dang/ /thabs ni gnyis med gang zhig lha mi lha min gyis bstod dang po'i sangs rgyas de la 'dud/ /ye
2b5(rgyud 'grel): shes stong nyid ye shes kyis/ /legs dag rnam dag 'gyur ba med/ /sems ni mtshan med ye shes kyis/ /legs dag gnyis med tshes bdag
3a1(rgyud 'grel): nyid/ /ngag ni smon med ye shes kyis/ /dag pa gsang sngags mi bzad sgra/ /de bzhin mngon par 'dus ma byas/ /ye shes kyis dag dri ma med/ /shes
3a2(rgyud 'grel): rab thabs kyis bdag nyid sbyor/ /dbyibs sku rdzu 'phrul bgrod pa can/ /de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje sems/ /byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' che/ /dam tshig sems
3a3(rgyud 'grel): dpa' gsung ba gang/ /dngos dang dngos med zad pa'i gtso/ /thog mdza' med cing zhi ba yi/ /byang chub sems de la phyag 'tshal/ /sprul pa yi ni sku gsung thugs/ /
3a4(rgyud 'grel): ye shes gcig sbyor sdom pa dang/ /longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku gsung thugs/ /ye shes gcig sbyor sdom pa dang/ /dpal ldan chos kyi sku gsung thugs/ /ye shes
3a5(rgyud 'grel): gcig sbyor sdom pa dang/ /lhan cig skyes pa'i sku gsung thugs/ /ye shes gcig sbyor sdom pa ni/ /sad rmi gnyid stug bzhi pa yi/ /dbang po gnyis skyes bde min zhing/ /
3b1(rgyud 'grel): ye shes sems dang ngag dang lus/ /gnas gzhir yang dag mi gnas te/ /las kyi phyag rgya yongs dor zhing/ /ye shes phyag rgya rnam par spangs/ /phyag rgya che las yang dag skyes/ /lhan skyes gzhan dang 'grogs
3b2(rgyud 'grel): pa min/ /rnam rtog sgom pa las 'das pa/ phyag rgya chen po mi 'gyur bde/ /gzung dang 'dzin pa dbyibs dag dang/ /rtog dang brjod pa rnam par spangs/ /dri za'i grong khyer rnam pa dang/ /pra phab pa yi rang bzhin can/ /thabs
3b3(rgyud 'grel): dang shes rab bdag nyid sbyar/ /e baM yi ge de la 'dud/ /phra rab rdul gyis chos nyid 'das/ /pra phab pa yi rang bzhin can/ /rnam pa kun gyi mchog ldan ma/ /phyag rgya chen mo de la 'dud/ /sangs rgyas kun gyi skyed
3b4(rgyud 'grel): mdzad ma/ /skye ba dang ni 'jig pa spangs/ /kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa can/ /sna tshogs yum de la phyag 'tshal/ /A li kA li snyoms 'jug dang/ /hUM phaT yi ge sogs spangs kyang/ /'gyur ba med las 'khrungs pa'i
3b5(rgyud 'grel): sku/ /dus kyi 'khor lo de la 'dud/ /kun mkhyen ye shes sku zhes pa/ /khyab bdag nyi ma lta bu'i sku/ /pad+ma'i 'dab ma rgyas pa'i spyan/ /de nyid bcu drug dbye ba las/ /sku bzhi'i bdag nyid sangs rgyas ni/ /rdo rje seng ge'i
3b6(rgyud 'grel): gdan bzhugs pa/ /lha dang lha min gyis bstod sngon/ /zla bzang gis gsol de la 'dud/ /dag dang ye shes gcig sbyor rgyal ba mchog gi dam tshig thugs dang chos ni gcig tu sbyor/ /gsung dang longs spyod rdzogs
4a1(rgyud 'grel): pa gcig sbyor srid gsum gyis mchod sku dang sprul pa rnal 'byor te/ /shes dang shes bya gnyis med srid 'das 'byor pa 'di ni rdo rje sems dpa' rnam pa bzhi/ /rdo rje'i rnal 'byor
4a2(rgyud 'grel): thabs dang shes rab bdag nyid lha mi lha min gyis bstod de la 'dud/ /zhabs gcig rdo rje nor bur rdul dang nyi ma dang/ /gnyis pa gtsug tor khu ba ri bong can la ni/ /rtag tu mi chod dbyer
4a3(rgyud 'grel): med 'dod par bkod gyur pa/ /'jig rten gsum gyis mchod pa'i gtso la spyi bos 'dud/ /rlung me chu dang sa yi dkyil 'khor lhun po pad+ma dang/ /zla nyid dus me'i steng du dbang phyug dang ni bdud
4a4(rgyud 'grel): kyi mgor/ /zhabs ni srid pa'i yum gyi zhabs dang lhan cig bkod gyur pa/ /lha yi dbang pos btud pa'i gtso la spyi bos phyag 'tshal te/ /de ltar rdo rje'i rnal 'byor gang zhig dpag med
4a5(rgyud 'grel): bde gshegs rnams kyi rten cing bstan pa dang/ /byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje mchog 'dzin gsang sngags rig pa kun gyis yang dag brjod gyur pa'i/ /'gyur med mchog gi bde ba rnal
4a6(rgyud 'grel): 'byor de ni dus kyi 'khor lor blun po bdag brjod 'dod/ /mkha' la myur 'gro mkha' 'gro'i bdag po 'gro ste 'dabs chags gzhan pa 'gro ba min nam ci/ /gang du rang gi lus la srid pa mdza' 
4b1(rgyud 'grel): dag sngags bcas pa/ /gsal bar a li thig le 'dzin pa'i rgyal ba'i dbang pos gsungs/ /chu gter chen po der ni rgyal ba'i slad du rab zhugs pa/ /de la gal te pha rol bdag phyin rgyal ba'i mthu yin no/ /gang phyir gsang bdag la gsung
4b2(rgyud 'grel): mchog gi dang po'i sangs rgyas las/ /stobs bcu pa yis bsdus pa'i rgyud ni sngon du lung bstan pa/ /de phyir dus kyi 'khor lo bsdus pa'i rgyud 'di ka lA phar/ /'jam dpal gyis ni thub pa mdza' dag rnams la nges par bstan/ /'grel bshad stong phrag drug cu pa/ /
4b3(rgyud 'grel): zla ba bzang pos bris pa gang/ /theg pa kun don gsal byed de/ /pad+ma dkar po bdag gis ni/ /rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi rjes 'jug cing/ /gzhung ni stong phrag bcu gnyis te/ /rdo rje'i tshig 'byed dang bcas pa/ /bsdus pa'i rgyud la bri bar bya/ /rgyal bas gsungs
4b4(rgyud 'grel): pa'i cho gas dbang mchog blangs nas rgyud 'di 'am ni bsdus pa yis/ /rgyud rgyal ma lus thos nas yang dag ye shes lam la gnas pa'i rnal 'byor pas/ /khengs dang longs spyod 'byor pa du ma btang nas sems ni bla mar gtang bya ste/ /sangs rgyas
4b5(rgyud 'grel): nyid kyi slad du gtso bo'i 'grel bshad gzhan phan spyod pa mnyan par bya/ /mngon shes med gang dpal ldan rdo rje theg pa la gnas brtan bcos du ma yis/ /rnam rtog chos kyi snying dang mkhas pa nyid kyi dregs ldan 'grel bshad chen po dag /byed
4b6(rgyud 'grel): pa de ni glang chen long ba myos bzhin dgra yis rgyu ni brgyal ba'i slad/ /gang gnas de yis rang gi rgyud ni nyams byed 'di ni rtag tu bdud kyi gnyen/ /mkhas pa'i mngon pa'i nga rgyal dang ldan rgyal bdag gsung ni mi shes dang tshul
4b7(rgyud 'grel): rtag longs pas/ /theg mchog 'grel bshad byas te long ba bzhan dag lhung du bcus nas dmyal bar rab 'jug pa/ /'gyod pa dang ni srog gcod la sogs mi dge'i las la bud med bde bas sems drangs shing/ /dpal
5a1(rgyud 'grel): ldan shes rab bde nyams rdo rje'i tshig bcom phyi yi longs spyod dag gis zil mnan pa'o/ /ston pa nyid kyis rgyal bdag bde ster rdo rje theg par gang zhig lung bstan mdza' dag ni/ /'grel bshad dag dang bsdu ba mdzad pa rdo rje mchog 'dzin bdag 'dra'i
5a2(rgyud 'grel): byang chub sems dpa' ste/ /de dag 'dir ni lha dang lag 'gro mi rnams smin pa'i don du sangs rgyas mthu smra la/ /gang dag mngon shes lnga med de dag bdag cag rgyal dbang yin zhes bden pa min par smra/ /ma 'ongs dus na rtag tu rtog ge la sogs bstan bcos la gtad
5a3(rgyud 'grel): sna tshogs bla/ /sangs rgyas pa yang gzhan gyi rtog ge dang phrad dbang gis log pa 'byung 'gyur te/ /rtog ge la gtad de yis 'dod pa'i yul la lam ni ston par byed pa gang/ /de dag nyid kyi blo ngan skyon ni 'joms byed 'grel bshad bdag gis bri bar bya/ /chags
5a4(rgyud 'grel): bral med pa'i 'dod chags mdza' yas chu la zhe sdang sbrul dang chu srin dkrigs/ /gti mug klong ni rab mang 'gro 'ong nor dang dpal la brkam pa'i rba rlabs can/ /'gyod sogs bsod pa la sogs las kyi rta gdong 'khor mo sgra drag srid pa yi/ /chu gter la ni
5a5(rgyud 'grel): dpal ldan rdo rje theg pa'i 'grel bshad rtag tu mnyan pa ste/ /shes rab rlung gi dar gyis myur 'gro myang 'das pha rol don gnyer chen po rnams/ /dam pa'i bde bas myur du rgal bar byed slad de ni lam gyi 'dren ma dang/ /nyon mongs bdud tshogs 'joms pa mkhas pa'i
5a6(rgyud 'grel): yang dag ye shes yid bzhin nor bu ste/ 'jig rten gsum gyi bdag po nyid ster 'di ni kun tu ston par byed pa'o/ /gang zhig phung po la sogs sgrib pa rab bcom yul ni pra phab brgyad lta bu/ /kun mkhyen bde ster de nyid gcig pu rdo rje 'dzin pa'i phyag rgya chen
5a7(rgyud 'grel): mo ste/ /de bor sangs rgyas nyid slad nor la chags shing 'khyogs pa'i snying ldan brtags ma dang/ /gang gi sten byed rnam brtags blo can de yis de yang 'pho ba thob par byed/ /'dod chags nyams las sdig ste gang phyir shin tu sdug ma las ni zhe sdang skye/ /sdang
5b1(rgyud 'grel): las gti mug 'di las rang gi rdo rje lhung las sems ni rtag smongs te/ /mchog min ma lus bza' dang btung ba la sogs yul gzhan dag la rab tu 'jug /de yi sems la co 'dris bde ba nyams shing skye ba drug tu 'khor bar 'gyur/ /kun mkhyen lam don gnyer ba
5b2(rgyud 'grel): rtsams la sgra dang sgra min rnam dpyad chen po med/ /sna tshogs yul skad ngan pa yis kyang chen po rnams kyi lam la rtag tu 'jug /sems can rnams kyi mos pa'i sems kyi dbang gis thams cad mkhyen pa'i gsung gzhan la/ /lung ston dag la lha klus bkod pa'i sgra sogs
5b3(rgyud 'grel): rtsod pa don gnyer rnams kyi gzhan/ /yul gyi skad dang zur chag sgra las kyang rnal 'byor ldan pas don ni 'dzin byed de/ /chu la 'o ma nges par zhugs pa ste/ /dad pas rab tu phyung nas 'thung bar byed/ /don dam de nyid yul la rtag tu ni/ /chen po rnam dag tshig la ston
5b4(rgyud 'grel): pa min/ /yul gyi ming rnams kyis ni don shes la/ /bstan bcos sgra dag gis ni ci zhig bya/ /gang zhig zur chag sgra dang sgrar gyur pas/ /brjod pa de nyid ye shes ma yin zhing/ /gang zhig 'gro ba dag la nyi tshe ba/ /de ni thams cad mkhyen pa'i gsung ma yin/ /mchog
5b5(rgyud 'grel): tu mi 'gyur bzhi pa de nyid ni/ /sangs rgyas rnams kyi shes rab ye shes te/ /gang zhig de ni slar yang de bzhin 'di/ /rang gi phyag rgya chen mor rgyal bas gsungs/ /shes rab 'grog la gang gis dkar po zab/ /de'i bde ba ci yis 'phel bar 'gyur/ /dpyid dang
5b6(rgyud 'grel): 'grogs la me tog ma rgyas pa/ /lhung ba tsu ta'i 'bras bu ci yis 'byung/ /gang gi 'gyur med ma thob sdug bsngal can/ /de ni 'gyur ba dang bcas bde ba tshol/ /thams cad chu ni tshol byed tsA ta ka /skom par gyur kyang sa la gnas pa min/ /'khor ba yi ni bde ba
5b7(rgyud 'grel): mi rtag pa/ /'thob pa min yang rmongs chen tshol bar byed/ /yang dag rgyal srid bde ba thob pa yang/ /thar pa'i don du mkhas pas 'dor bar byed/ /ji ltar lo yi mtshams su rgya lam na/ /ri dags zas can 'khrig pa'i bde ba tshol/ /rdo yi bye ma dag gi kha zas
6a1(rgyud 'grel): can/ /phug ron rnams ni rtag tu byed pa ste/ /lan cig rtag tu khu ba lhung ba'i phyir/ /gnyis ka la yang mchog gi bde ba med/ /de bzhin dka' thub can dang 'od ldan la/ /rmi lam sad pa dag las mdzag phyir ro/ /ji ltar gnyid log la yang
6a2(rgyud 'grel): sprul gyi ni/ /sa btab mi 'tsho de bzhin dka' thub pa/ /khu ba sdud pa med phyir stobs med ma'i/ /skye gnas de yis nyams bar byed pa'o/ /ji ltar rdo dreg skud pa'i gos dag ni/ /me yi sregs pa nyid kyi dag 'gyur ba/ /de bzhin skyes bu rnams kyi dam pa yi/ /sems
6a3(rgyud 'grel): ni shes rab ye shes dag gis so/ /ji ltar dngul chu me yi reg pa las/ /'bros par byed kyi g.yo ba med mi 'gyur/ /de bzhin thabs dang bral ba'i khu ba ni/ /rtag tu skye gnas reg pa dag las so/ /ji ltar g.yo ba de yang smon sogs kyi/ /stobs kyi me dang yang dag
6a4(rgyud 'grel): phrad bas 'ching/ /de bzhin khu ba shin tu rnal 'byor gyis/ /shes rab dag dang yang dag phrad pas so/ /ji ltar me ni shing la rtags nas kyang/ /bcad dang dbye ba'i thabs kyi mi mthong ste/ /gtsubs shing gtsubs stan lag pas bsrubs pa las/ /de la gnas pa
6a5(rgyud 'grel): dag kyang mthong gyur pa/ /de bzhin sems kyi 'od gsal rtog pa yi/ /sgom pa'i thabs rnams dag gis mi mthong ste/ /de nyid du 'di rkyang ma dag dang ni/ /ro ma gcig tu sbyor bas mthong bar 'gyur/ /sna tshogs rnam rtog la sogs lam gyis ni/ /de nyid de
6a6(rgyud 'grel): bzhin gshegs pas gang gsungs pa/ /bcu drug bzhi yis rab tu dbye ba can/ /lam dang bral ba 'thob pa ma yin no/ /bskyed pa'i rim par gsungs pa'i hUM dang ni/ /phaT yig la sogs rtog pa dang bral ba/ /rdzogs pa'i rim pa'i rnal 'byor de nyid de/ /
6a7(rgyud 'grel): de nyid kyi ni sgrub thabs gzhan yid min/ /du ba la sogs mtshan ma dag dang ni/ /srog rtsol dag gis dbu mar 'phab pa dang/ /rig ma'i rtul zhugs dag gis rdo rje ni/ /ltung min de bzhin steng du zhu ba ste/ /lam 'di dag gis sangs rgyas rnams kyi ni/ /bde
6b1(rgyud 'grel): ba mchog tu 'gyur ba med pa zhes/ /mngon par brjod pa 'am pho nya mo kun gyi/ /lhan cig skyes pa rnal 'byor pas thob 'gyur/ /gzugs la sogs par rdog pa dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lo bsgom pa goms par gyur pas ni/ /grub pa 'jig rten pa dag 'grub 'gyur te
6b2(rgyud 'grel): 'dod pa'i dngos grub chen po ga la zhig /gang zhig sems can rnams la brtse ba yis/ /gzhan don dge la rtag tu brtson pa yis/ /slob ma dag pa rnams la lam dag ni/ /bla ma dam pa'i drin las 'byung ba yin/ /lam bzang rin chen 'di ni bag med kyi/ /sems
6b3(rgyud 'grel): can gzhan pa dag la byin pa na/ /rang khyim dgon pa dag tu rab zhugs la/ /yul ngan chom rkun rnams kyis 'phrog par byed/ /the tshom 'gyod pa dag dang gnyid dang ni/ /le lo rgod pa'i chom rkun rnams kyis kyang/ /gnyen 'dun thibs po'i nang du zhugs pa yi/ /lam
6b4(rgyud 'grel): bzang rin chen dag ni 'phrog par byed/ /srog gcod ma byin gzhan gyi bud med dang/ /rdzun dang tshig rtsub dag dang phra ma dang/ /'khyal par gyur pa'i tshig dang brnab sems dang/ /gnod sems lta ba ngan pa'i chom rkun dang/ /yod pa'i sdig dang nye bar sdig pa dang/ /
6b5(rgyud 'grel): gsod khu dbang po mngon par zhen pa ste/ /chom rkun lnga pa lnga po 'di dag gis/ /rin po che yi rtag tu 'phrog par byed/ /shin tu bza' dang btung ba sna tshogs dang/ /longs spyod du ma'i chom rkun de dag gis/ /brtson 'grus ldan du zin kyang bag med cing/ /rgyal bar
6b6(rgyud 'grel): gyur pa nyid la 'phrog par byed/ rang nyid kyis ni yongs su ma brtags par/ /rin thang chen por gyur pa yin ma yin/ /shes par bya phyir g.yon can gzhan la ston/ /de yi tshig gis rin chen 'dod par byed/ /gang dag rin chen bzang po rig pa rnams/ /rin chen chen po
6b7(rgyud 'grel): yongs su rtog du bzhugs/ /de dag rnams kyi rnam dag tshig gis ni/ /rang gi rin chen rnam par shes par bya/ /rdzogs sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems rnams dang/ /pha dang ma dang bu mo srid mo dang/ /bu dang spun zla 'dod pa'i chung ma yi/ /gzugs rnams dag gis
7a1(rgyud 'grel): bdud ni gegs byed do/ /de phyir bla ma dam pas gnang ba yi/ /lam bzang rin chen dag ni slob ma yis/ /chom rkun rtsa lag yongs su btang byas te/ /'bad pas shin tu legs par sba bar bya/ /dpa' bo'i rim pa dag byin brlab pa yi/ /rim pa
7a2(rgyud 'grel): dag kyang thar pa'i lam ma yin/ /shin tu rnam dag rim pa gcig po ni/ /thar pa'i slad du sangs rgyas rnams kyis bstan/ /mtshams med lnga po dag ni byas pa rnams/ /dbang don bde ba nyid ni gang zhig gis/ /thabs dang shes rab bdag nyid rgyud
7a3(rgyud 'grel): dag la/ /rgyal ba'i dbang pos yang dag bzung bar 'gyur/ /dpa' bo'i rim pa phyi rol la min te/ /lus la srog zad nyid la 'di gsungs so/ /bdag byin brlab pa dag ni stong pa la/ /khams gsum po ni mthong bar gyur pa'i mtshan/ /'khor ba'i
7a4(rgyud 'grel): snying po med de zad gyur pa/ /de las skyes pa'i sangs rgyas nyid 'bras te/ /chu shing gi ni 'bras bu smin pa dag /chu shing nyams pas yang dag 'byung ba bzhin/ /sdig pa dang ni shing srin sems can rnams/ /gang las byung ba de dag de nyams
7a5(rgyud 'grel): byed/ /de bzhin rnal 'byor dag gis sems de ni/ /sgyu ma rnam par nyams par byed pa yin/ /gnyis med g.yo ba med dang rig med dang/ /'dod dang mchog tu mi 'gyur 'dod chags che/ /dngos dang dngos po med pa med pa dang/ /ye shes
7a6(rgyud 'grel): dang ni sems dpa' kun tu bzang/ /nyon mongs med dang nyon mongs chen po dang/ /lhan skyes dpal ldan byang sems thig le 'dzin/ /dpal ldan dus kyi 'khor lo rdo rje dang/ /thabs dang shes rab bdag nyid rnal 'byor ro/ /snying rje dang ni stong
7a7(rgyud 'grel): nyid sku/ /dus ni kun rdzob gzugs can ma/ /stong nyid 'khor lo zhes brjod de/ /dus kyi 'khor lo gnyis med 'dod/ /'di yi dpal ni myur thob slad/ /rtag tu rnal 'byor ma rnams zhabs/ /rnal 'byor gang zhig bsgom pa de'i/ /bgegs
7b1(rgyud 'grel): ni rtag tu nyams par 'gyur/ /dgra dang seng ge glang chen dbang po me dang ltos 'gro'i bdag dang chom rkun zhags pas 'ching/ /chu gter 'khrug dang sha za 'chi ba'i 'jigs byed nad dang dbang po'i nye bar 'tshe ba dang/ /dbul dang bud med dang bral mi bdag 'khrugs pa'i 'jigs
7b2(rgyud 'grel): dang rdo rje ltung dang nor nyams rnams/ /gang zhig rnal 'byor ma rnams zhabs ni gsal bar dran byed de la rab tu nyams par 'gyur/ /glang chen shing rta rta dang rab tu mang ba'i mi mchog thams cad lus la go bgos shing/ /lag la mdung dang 'khor lo ral gri mda'
7b3(rgyud 'grel): gzhu dgra rnams kyis ni g.yul du 'joms byed pa/ /'chi ster drag po'i gzugs can phyogs dang mtshams son dgra ste thams cad rang gi mtshon gyis ni/ /bcom ldan rgyal ba'i grags pa gang zhig rnal 'byor ma rnams zhabs dran byed pas kun nas
7b4(rgyud 'grel): 'thob/ /kun nas seng ge'i sgra sgrogs shin tu rnam par 'gyur ba'i gzhi ldan mche ba rnon po gtsigs/ /rnga ma g.yo zhing sder mo gug la brtan pas glang chen myos pa'i glad pa rab tu 'gems/ /rab khros nyi ma 'char ka'i mig can ro
7b5(rgyud 'grel): 'dzin ral gri g.yo ba'i gsod 'dod ral pa can/ /gang gis rnal 'byor ma rnams zhabs dag 'jigs 'brog dran pa de la ring du 'gro bar 'gyur/ /mdog sngo mig ni ser skya 'gram pa gnyis po myos pa'i chu bo rab tu mang bas gang/ rnam
7b6(rgyud 'grel): mang ljon pa mchog rnams rtsad nas 'byin cing rab tu grugs byed 'brug bzhin sgra dag sgrogs/ /lag pas bcing ba byas nas so yi rtse mo dag gis 'byed byed rab mchog glang po'i bdag /gang gis rnal 'byor ma rnams zhabs dag 'jigs
7b7(rgyud 'grel): 'phrog dran pa de yi lus ni gtong bar byed/ /kun nas me lce rab 'bar phyogs dang mtshams su du ba kun gyis mun pa chen po gtibs/ /grong dang dgon pa dus cig sreg cing skar mda' ltung ba bzhin du me stag spro bar byed/ /
8a1(rgyud 'grel): sems can rnams la dus kun du ni pA chi ga'i 'jigs byed phyogs kun khyab par gyur pa'i me/ /gang gi rnal 'byor ma rnams khabs dag 'jigs 'phrog dran pa de la bsil pa nyid du 'gyur/ /khros shing mig sman sngon po'i mdog dang
8a2(rgyud 'grel): 'khyog por bgrod pa'i lus can drag po'i phugs sgra sgrogs/ /mche ba 'khyog po lce gnyis dad ldan 'chi ba'i 'jigs byed rlung gi gzugs can rab tu gtum/ /drag po'i mig dang ge dang ka gsal byas yang dag phrad pa za par byed pa'i gdengs can dbang//
8a3(rgyud 'grel): gang gis rnal 'byor ma rnams zhabs dag 'jigs 'phrogs dran pa de la rab tu nyams par 'gyur/ /sdang ba'i sems ldan lag pa'i mthil na gzhu dang rna ba'i bar du mnga' bkad mdung dang ni/ /'khor lo ral gri lag thogs phyogs dang mtshams su gnas
8a4(rgyud 'grel): pas dam pa'i lam gyi sa bkag nas/ /dgon par lam 'gron skye bo rgyu ba dang phrad 'joms byed drag po'i mig can chom rkun pa/ /gang gi rnal 'byor ma rnams zhabs dag 'jigs 'phrog dran pa de la ring ba nyid du 'gyur/ /lag pa dag ni zhags
8a5(rgyud 'grel): pas bcings shing rkang pa'i pad+ma zung ni lcags sgrog dag gis gtams/ /dge ba'i chu dang bral bas lce dang mgrin pa chu skams lus po skem zhing bgres pas bzing/ /nyin mtshan dus su rje bo khros pa'i bka' yis kun du srung ma rnams kyis srung
8a6(rgyud 'grel): byed pa/ /gang gi rnal 'byor ma rnams zhabs dag 'jigs 'phrog dran pa de yang de las grol bar 'gyur/ /chu gter gzhon pa la zhon mdza' yas drag po'i rlung gi chu yi gter ni 'khrug byed cing/ /kun tu 'khod bar byed la chu gter chom rkun
8a7(rgyud 'grel): chu srin nya yi rigs kyis bkag gyur te/ /me yi til mar gdug pas 'phangs pa me yi char chen kun nas rgyun du 'bab pa la/ /gang gis rnal 'byor ma rnams zhabs dag 'jigs 'phrog bran pa de yang na las pha rol 'gro/ phaT ces 'jigs
8b1(rgyud 'grel): rung sgra sgrogs kha nas me 'bar lag na gri gug dang ni thod pa thogs/ ro langs gdug pa'i sems ldan phyogs bcu'i dkyil 'khor dag la yang dag gnas shing 'jigs par byed/ bkres pas gzir te sha dag za zhing mi khrag la dga' lus skams gos dang bral ba
8b2(rgyud 'grel): dus de gang gi rnal 'byor ma rnams zhabs dag 'jig 'phrog dran pa de la srung bar byed par 'gyur/ /nyin bzhin 'khun zhing sor mo'i rtse mo zlum po nyams te sna dang mchu dang rna ba nyams/ /gdong dang mgrin pa rkang lag dag gi rma rnams las ni rnag rul mang po drag dang
8b3(rgyud 'grel): tu? lag /rul pa'i dri pa'i mthu las gnyen pa shes tshogs kyi shi ba'i lus bzhin yongs su btang gyur pa/ /gang zhig rnal 'byor ma rnams zhabs bzang dran byed nas kyis btang zhing 'dod dang ldan par 'gyur/ /'bar bcas mche gnon gdengs can 'brog bya
8b4(rgyud 'grel): sha ba d+ha dang stag dang glang chen gdod ldan zhing/ /lag na 'khor lo ral gri mda' dang rtse gsum lcags kyu rdo rje thogs pas phyogs kun tu/ /byang chub bsam gtan gcig gzhol mchog bde la gnas sgrub pa po bsdigs dang dpo'i pho nya gang/ /de dag rnal 'byor dbang
8b5(rgyud 'grel): phyug ma zhabs gang gis rang yid la byed de la nyams par 'gyur/ /dbyar ni nags nas grong gi bar du 'dam rdzab kyis gang lam dag la yang khur khyer zhing/ /dgun ni gos dang bral bas kha ba'i lam du bgrod cing yul gzhan dag tu 'ang 'gro bar byed/ /so ga chu med
8b6(rgyud 'grel): 'jigs bcas mya ngan lam du nyi ma'i 'od zer gyis gdungs dbul po gang/ /rnal 'byor ma rnams zhabs bzang sgom byed sdug bsngal de dag gis btang 'dod dang ldan par 'gyur/ /mchan khung mig dang rna ba sna dang kha lus brjod pa dag las mi bzang dri
8b7(rgyud 'grel): 'byung zhing/ /bud med kun dang bral bas dus kun tu ni dga' ba'i bde ba dang bral skal ngan te/ /mi dge 'bras bu'i dbang gis rtag tu bud med sdang bar gyur pa gang la de dag kun/ /rnal 'byor ma rnams zhabs ni bde ba mchog sbyin bsgoms pas bskal bzang kha
9a1(rgyud 'grel): dog gzugs can 'gyur/ /'khus phyir g.yog 'khor dang la mi dbang 'khrugs te 'jigs pa'i gshin rje lta bur mdza' cig tu/ /gsod pa la zhen 'chi ba'i 'jigs pa byed pa'i sde rnams yang dag myur du sku la byed pa/ /rnal 'byor ma
9a2(rgyud 'grel): rnams zhabs ni 'jig rten gsum po kun gyi mgon dag rang yid la bsgoms pas/ /de dag rnams kyis de yang rab tu zhi zhing 'dod pa thams cad sbyin pas mchog sbyin 'gyur/ /gang dag 'ga' zhig tu ni nam mkha' las rdo rje rab ltung bud med 'grogs las
9a3(rgyud 'grel): rtag par yang/ /skye dang skye ba gzhan slad 'chi dang rgyal dang chags bral slar yang byed pas rnal 'byor ma'i/ /dpal ldan las dang ye shes mchog gi chu skyes la gnas rdo rje'i zhabs dag bsgoms pa yis/ /de dag rnams kyi de yang rab zhi 'chil
9a4(rgyud 'grel): nyid 'gyur slar yang skye ba ldan pa min/ /gang dag nyin dang mtshan mor bud med 'grogs la rnam par chags pas nor kun nyams 'gyur zhing/ /skye ba gzhan gyi bag chags bgos pa'i sems las de ni slar yang mang po rab 'byung bas/ /shes rab
9a5(rgyud 'grel): rnal 'byor ma rnams dag gi mi mnyam mnyam pa'i zhabs ni sna tshogs gzugs can gang/ /rgyal ba mchog gis mchod cing bstod pa bsgoms pas de ni nor kun nyams par mi 'gyur ro/ /ser skya lug dang kun 'dar ma ste nyi zla sgra gcan lam gsum
9a6(rgyud 'grel): bgrod rnams rnal 'byor ma/ /dngos dang dngos med rab nyams mnyam bgrod zhabs de dag ni de dag rnams kyi ye shes sku/ /de yi lhan skyes bde ba'i go 'phang 'gyur med cig 'di de dag de nyid gang gis dran/ /de yi skye ba 'di la ma lus 'jigs
9a7(rgyud 'grel): 'phrog 'dir brjod 'bras bu myur du 'byung bar 'gyur/ /dpal ldan rnal 'byor ma rnams dag gis rdo rje nor bu'i khyim ni gnas te der 'jug lam/ /nyon mongs med cing bdud nyams sngon du rgyal bas gsungs pa'i bstod pa bdag gis 'dir brjod do/ /
9b1(rgyud 'grel): skyes bu gang dag bdud kyis grogs kyis rtag tu mi bden mun par song zhing lam nyams pa/ /de dag rnams kyis lam 'di thob nas rdo rje nor bu'i khyim dang ring min 'ong gyur cig /ngu ba la sogs lam gyi lhan skyes pa'i bde ba'i go 'phang bsgoms nas de
9b2(rgyud 'grel): ni dus 'khor lo/ /sum cu rtsa gnyis mtshan gyi yan lag 'gro ba'i bla ma chos kyi 'khor lo 'di la gnas/ /lha gnas mgo yi gtsug gi nor bu'i 'od zer tshogs kyi zhabs kyi pad+ma la gtugs shing/ /dam pa'i lam ni ston byed nyin mor byed pa bzhin
9b3(rgyud 'grel): du mun pa thams cad 'joms par 'gyur/ /lha klu mi dang lha min dbang po'i cod pan dag gis zhabs pad la gtugs gang/ /yang dag ye shes nyin byed 'gro ba gsum gyi dpal ldan chos kyi 'khor lor gnas/ /bdud dang nyon mongs ri dwags rab gtum gsod byed
9b4(rgyud 'grel): dpal ldan shAkya seng ge de'i/ /rtag tu 'grol brtse dang de yi shes rab kyis bskul 'grel bshad bdag gis bris/ /kA yig las ni sgyu zhi ba/ /la yig 'di la thim pa nyid/ /tsa yig gis ni g.yo ba'i sems/ /kra yig rim pa bcings las so/ /dus ni 'gyur
9b5(rgyud 'grel): med bde ye shes/ /thabs dang snying rje'i bdag nyid de/ /'khor lo shes bya'i rnam 'gro dpal/ /shes rab stong nyid bdag nyid do/ /'di ni dpal ldan dus 'khor lo/ /rdo rje rnal 'byor thams cad nas/ /bden pa gnyis la gnas pa 'di/ /mngon par brjod
9b6(rgyud 'grel): pa'i rjod byed 'gyur/ /bde bar gshegs pas lung bstan cing/ /'jam dpal gyis ni skul gyur pa/ /'jig rten mgon po bdag gis ni/ /rgyud 'di'i 'grel bshad bri bar bya/ /byis pa mkhas pa rmongs rnams la/ /rgyud
9b7(rgyud 'grel): kyi gsad pa'i gsal byed de/ /ma yi bu la phan pa bzhin/ /lus can thams cad bde don du'o/ /rdo rje sems dpa' lam mchog ni/ /gang gi rnal 'byor pas rig byed/ /de phyir dri ma med pa'i 'od/ /'grel bshad 'di ni myur du dri/ /bsdus pa'i rgyud
10a1(rgyud 'grel): kyi rgyal bo dus kyi 'khor lo'i 'grel bshad rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi rjes su 'jug pa stong phrag bcu gnyis pa dri ma med pa'i 'od ces bya ba las bdud dang bgegs mdza' dag nyams par byed pa/ mchog gi 'dod pa'i lha dang/ dam pa'i
10a2(rgyud 'grel): lam nges pa'i mdor bsdus chen po ste dang po'o// //'dir dang por re zhig rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi rjes su 'brangs te brjod bya dang brjod byed dang 'brel pa la sogs pa dang bsdus pa'i rgyud la sogs pa lung bstan pa brjod par bya
10a3(rgyud 'grel): ste /phyi nas bsdus pa'i rgyud la dgos pa dang/ dgos pa'i dgos pa la sogs pa yang ngo/ /'di la dang por re zhig brjod bya dang rjod byed dang 'brel pa dang/ dgos pa dang dgos pa'i dgos pa rnams mngon par gzigs nas/ gdul bya'i skye bo
10a4(rgyud 'grel): nges pa dang bral ba rnams la rang gi sems kyi bsam pas skye ba 'di la sangs rgyas nyid kyi 'bras bu rab tu ster ba/ bde ba chen po'i gnas mchog gi dang po'i sangs rgyas rdo rje dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor chen por rdo rje seng ge'i khri la bzhugs pa sangs
10a5(rgyud 'grel): rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' dang khro bo'i rgyal po dang lha dang klu dang lha dang lha mo'i tshogs kyis yongs su bskor ba/ khams gsum pas zhabs kyi padmo la phyag byas pa/ khams gsum gyi 'khor lo sgyur ba/ mchog gi dang po'i sangs rgyas rigs med
10a6(rgyud 'grel): pa/ bcom ldan 'das dpal dus kyi 'khor lo la/ zla ba bzang pos gsol ba btab par gyur pa yis/ mchog gi dang po'i sangs rgyas stong phrag bcu gnyis pa/ rigs med pa rgyud kyi rgyal po dus kyi 'khor lo/ rdo rje 'dzin pa'i ye shes kyi sku mngon
10a7(rgyud 'grel): du gyur pa'i mtshan yang dag par brjod pas 'khyud pa/ rgyud thams cad kyi rdo rje'i tshig mngon du gyur pa/ sangs rgyas rin chen za ma gtog kha 'byed pa/ 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i bden pa la brten pa/ rdzogs pa'i byang chub pa rnam pa bzhi dang
10b1(rgyud 'grel): rdo rje rnam pa bzhi yongs su dag pa/ sku bzhi dang/ rigs drug dang/ bden pa bcu gnyis dang/ de kho na nyid bcu drug dang/ stong pa nyid bcu drug dang/ snying rje bcu drug gi bdag nyid kyis brjod par bya ba rjod par byed pa/ dbang skur ba 'jig rten pa'i bcu dang/ 'jig rten las
10b2(rgyud 'grel): 'das pa'i bcu gcig pa rab tu gsal bar byed pa las kyi phyag rgya dang/ ye shes kyi phyag rgya dang/ phyag rgya chen mo dang/ 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dngos grub rab tu gsal bar byed pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams dang/ nang dang/ mngon par dbang
10b3(rgyud 'grel): bskur ba dang/ sgrub thabs dang ye shes de/ le'u lnga'i bdag nyid dang/ brtag pa lnga'i bdag nyid ni/ mi la sogs pa'i sems can mdza' dag gis yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas nyid thob par bya ba'i phyir yang dag par bstan to/ /de las bsdus pa'i
10b4(rgyud 'grel): rgyud yang dag par sdud par byed pa la 'jam dpal dang/ ma 'ongs pa'i dus su tshangs pa'i drang srong rnams gdul bar bya ba'i don du 'grel bshad byed pa la bdag dang/ rgyud ston pa'i don du gshin rje mthar byed la sogs pa gzhan rnams dang/ sham b+ha la'i
10b5(rgyud 'grel): yul la sogs pa grong khyer bye ba phrag dgu bcu rtsa drug na gnas pa'i sems can thams cad dam pa'i lam thob pa la de bzhin gshegs pas lung bstan to/ /'dir rdul phra rab 'dus pa sngon du 'gro ba ni 'jig rten gyi khams so/ /'jig rten gyi khams sngon
10b6(rgyud 'grel): du 'gro ba ni sems can rnams so/ /sems can sngon du 'gro ba ni 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i mngon par dbang bskur ba'o/ /mngon par dbang bskur ba sngon du 'gro ba ni bsod nams kyi tshogs dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lo bsgoms pa goms pas
10b7(rgyud 'grel): 'og min gyi srid pa'i mthar thug pa 'jig rten pa'i dngos grub bsgrub pa'o/ /'jig rten pa'i dngos grub sngon du 'gro ba ni/ bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs dag dang skye ba snga ma'i stong pa nyid dang snying rje kun rdzob dang dmigs pa med pa'i bag chags
11a1(rgyud 'grel): kyi stobs kyis rdul phra rab 'dus pa las 'das shing/ dkyil 'khor la sogs pa rnam par rtog pa'i sgom pa dang bral ba phyag rgya chen po'i ye shes kyi dngos grub sgrub pa'o/ /de bas na dang por 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rtog pa'o/ /de nas nang gi brtag pa'o/
11a2(rgyud 'grel): de nas dbang bskur ba'i brtag pa'o/ /de nas 'jig rten pa'i dngos grub bsgrub pa'i brtag pa'o/ /de nas mchog tu mi 'gyur ba'i ye shes bsgrub pa'i brtag pa ste/ de ltar na rim pa ji lta ba bzhin rgyud kyi rgyal po ni brtag pa lnga'am le'u lnga'i bdag nyid do//
11a3(rgyud 'grel): 'dir thabs dang shes rab kyi bdag nyid rdo rje'i rnal 'byor dang po'i sangs rgyas rigs med pa bcom ldan 'das dus kyi 'khor lo ni brjod par bya'o/ /de yang le'u lnga po 'di'i ngo bo nyid kyi gnas te/ dang por re zhig 'jig rten gyi khams kyi le'u la/ /thams
11a4(rgyud 'grel): cad mkhyen pa zhes pa la sogs pa ston pa po'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ gnas brtan pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ 'khor chen po phun sum tshogs pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ gsol ba 'debs pa po'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ rdo rje'i
11a5(rgyud 'grel): rnal 'byor brjod par bya ba dang/ rjod par byed pa dang/ dgos pa'i dgos pa la sogs pa zhus pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ stong pa chen po yi ge lnga la sogs pa dang sna tshogs 'byung ba dang dkyil 'khor dang dbang bskur ba gsol ba 'debs pa'i
11a6(rgyud 'grel): ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ ston pa po'i lam gyi ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ 'jig rten gyi khams dang/ gza' dang/ rgyu skar dang/ sems can dang sngags dang srog la sogs pa 'byung ba dang sdud pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ rlung la
11a7(rgyud 'grel): sogs pa'i dkyil 'khor dang rgya mtsho dang gling dang ri'i grangs kyi ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ srid pa sum cu rtsa gcig gi ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ 'khor lo sgyur ba chen po 'byung ba'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ shin tu phra ba'i dbugs
11b1(rgyud 'grel): la sogs pa nyin mo'i tshad la sogs pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ 'jam dpal lung bstan pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ grub pa'i mdza' dang/ byed pa'i skar rtsis kyis ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ dbu ma'i rtsa'i dbugs rnams las gza'i rkang pa dang/
11b2(rgyud 'grel): rgyu skar gyi rkang pa skye ba'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ khyim bcu gnyis kyi gnas pas sa 'khor ba'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ dbyangs 'char ba la sogs pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ sgra gcan la sogs pa sa'i stobs kyi ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/
11b3(rgyud 'grel): rjod 'choms pa dang bsrung ba'i 'khrul 'khor gyi ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ 'khor los sgyur bas dum bu bcu gnyis su 'khor ba'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ kla klo'i chos bcom nas sangs rgyas kyi chos rab tu 'jog pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/
11b4(rgyud 'grel): sems can mdza' dag la 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dngos grub kyi lam 'das pa'i dngos grub lam sbyin pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ 'jam dpal dang/ 'jig rten dbang phyug sngon bdun dang phyi rgyab mar ston pa po'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa
11b5(rgyud 'grel): dang/ 'khor lo sgyur ba chen po la sogs pa rigs ldan gyi mthar thug par mi rnams mchog gi tshe'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa zhes bya ba ni 'jig rten gyi khams kyi le'u la'o// //de nas nang gi le'u la/ dang por
11b6(rgyud 'grel): mngal 'dzin pa dang sdud pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ rdul dang khu ba dang kun gzhi rnam par shes pa yang dag par sbyor ba'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ zla ba so so re re zhing mngal 'byung ba'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ nya la sogs pa gnas
11b7(rgyud 'grel): skabs bcu'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ sku bzhi dang rdo rje dag pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ rdzogs pa'i byang chub bzhis mngal 'byung ba'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ dbugs drug brgya lhag pa'i stong phrag nyi shu rtsa gcig dang/ rtsa stong phrag
12a1(rgyud 'grel): bdun cu rtsa gnyis dang/ tshigs kyi gnas sum brgya drug cu dang/ khams drug dang/ ro drug dang/ dbang po drug dang/ yul drug dang/ las kyi dbang po drug dang/ yul drug dang/ rnam par shes pa drug dang/ 'du byed drug dang/ tshor ba
12a2(rgyud 'grel): drug dang/ 'du shes drug dang/ gzugs drug dang/ ye shes drug dang/ 'khor lo drug dang/ dkyil 'khor drug steng dang 'og gi ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ lte ba'i chu skyes la sogs pa'i 'dab ma dang/ sna bug dag la g.yon dang g.yas kyi dkyil 'khor
12a3(rgyud 'grel): phung po lnga dang khams lnga 'bab pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ dbu ma la rgyud mdza' dag 'byung ba'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ srog la sogs pa rlung gi bya ba'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ khams rnams las lha'i mtshan ma 'byung ba'i ngo bo nyid
12a4(rgyud 'grel): kyis gnas pa dang/ nyi ma dang zla ba dang me'i 'chi ltas kyi ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ las kyi rnam par smin pas 'gro ba drug tu skye ba'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ rtsa la sogs pa gza' rkang pa 'chad pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ dbu mar
12a5(rgyud 'grel): zhugs pa'i dga' ba la sogs pa rnams kyi 'chi ltas kyi 'chi ba slu ba'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ phyi rol 'jig rten pa'i bya ba sgrub pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ lta ba thams cad rjes su dpag pas yongs su brtag pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa
12a6(rgyud 'grel): dang/ sems can sna tshogs kyi 'dod pa dang rjes su mthun par chos rab tu bzhag pa'i ngo bo nyid kyi gnas pa zhes bya ba ni nang gi le'u la'o// //de nas dbang gi le'u la/ dang por bla ma yongs su brtag pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/
12a7(rgyud 'grel): mchog dang 'bring dang tha ma'i slob ma yongs su brtags te bsdu ba'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ las rab 'byams bsgrub pa la grong la sogs pa'i phyogs kyi cha dang/ sa la sogs pa'i mtshan nyid kyi ngo bo nyid kyi gnas pa dang/ thabs khung dang/ sbyin sreg
12b1(rgyud 'grel): gi rdzas dang/ bgrang 'phreng dang/ gdan dang/ phur bu dang/ bum pa dang/ rdul tshon dang/ thig skud dang/ 'khrul 'khor dgod pa'i mtshan nyid kyi ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ sa yongs su bzung ba dang/ dkyil 'khor bri ba dang/ de nyid bcu yongs su shes pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang
12b2(rgyud 'grel): 'jig rten pa dang 'jig rten pa las 'das pa'i dbang sbyin pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ thams cad rab tu gnas pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ dam tshig gi 'khor lo 'dus pa dang/ dam tshig gi mchod pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ rigs gsum cu
12b3(rgyud 'grel): rtsa drug gi lha mo'i phyag rgya dang/ lta stangs dang mtshan dang dam tshig gi brda dang rigs la sogs pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lo gshegs su gsol ba'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ chu bo chen po la sogs pa dang rang rang gi khyim du rdul tshon
12b4(rgyud 'grel): dang tshogs kyi 'khor lo gshegs su gsol te/ mchod pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ dpal ldan bla ma dbul ba thams cad kyis mnyes pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa zhes bya ba ni dbang gi le'u la'o// //de nas sgrub thabs kyi le'u la/ dang por srung ba'i 'khor
12b5(rgyud 'grel): lo la sogs pa dang/ gdod dag pa dang/ rang gi snying ga'i zla ba'i sa bon gyi 'od zer rnams las de bzhin gshegs pa spro ba'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ bla na med pa'i mchod pa dang/ sdig pa bshags pa dang/ bsod nams la rjes su yi rang ba dang/ skyabs su 'gro ba gsum
12b6(rgyud 'grel): dang/ bdag nyid dbul ba dang/ byang chub tu sems bskyed pa dang/ lam bsten pa dang/ stong pa nyid la dmigs pa la sogs pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ bskyed pa'i rim pa la dkyil 'khor rgyal mchog dang las rgyal mchog dang/ thig le'i rnal 'byor dang phra mo'i rnal 'byor la sogs
12b7(rgyud 'grel): pa'i sgrub thabs kyi ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ phyi rol 'jig rten pa'i dngos grub kyi sgrub thabs kyi ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ mchod sbyin la sogs pa dang rig byed kyi mdza' gsang ba'i de kho na nyid kyi ye shes dang yan lag drug gi sbyor ba la sogs pa'i sgrub thabs kyi ngo bo 
13a1(rgyud 'grel): nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ sbyin pa la sogs pa bsod nams kyi tshogs kyi ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ mngon sum dang lkog du gyur pa'i sems bsgom pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa zhes bya ba ni sgrub thabs kyi le'u la'o// //de nas ye shes kyi
13a2(rgyud 'grel): le'u la/ dang por lus kyi rus pa la sogs pa'i khams rnam par dag pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ sku dang gsung dang thugs dang rigs drug gi lha'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ a la sogs pa dang ka la sogs pa sngags kyi rigs
13a3(rgyud 'grel): drug gi ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ thabs dang shes rab kyi rgyud sum cu rtsa drug gi ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ thabs dang shes rab dang bya ba dang rnal 'byor rjes su rig pa dang sdom pa chen po dang 'khor los sgyur ba drug spro ba'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang dbang bzhi
13a4(rgyud 'grel): pa mchog tu mi 'gyur ba phyag rgya chen po'i ye shes kyi dngos grub kyi sgrub thabs kyi ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor spro ba'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ byang chub kyi sems bsten pa'i sgrub thabs kyi ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ shes
13a5(rgyud 'grel): pa dang shes bya rnam pa kun gyi bdag nyid phyag rgya chen po'i dngos grub kyi ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ lus dang ngag dang sems kyi bya ba thams cad brtag pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ chos kyi phung po stong phrag brgyad cu rtsa bzhi bstan pa'i ngo bo nyid
13a6(rgyud 'grel): kyis gnas pa dang/ sangs rgyas gyi zhing bsdu ba'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ nam mkha' i khams la ri rab kyi rdul phra rab dang mnyam pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams dang thabs cig tu bzhugs pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ sangs rgyas kyi
13a7(rgyud 'grel): zhing 'byung ba'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing rdo rjer byin gyis brlabs pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ mos pa sna tshogs pa'i sems can gyi bsam pa'i dbang gis chos bstan pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang bcud dang bcud len pa la
13b1(rgyud 'grel): sogs pa lus kyi dngos grub kyi sgrub thabs kyi ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ mchog tu mi 'gyur ba'i bde bas sems can thams cad kyi don mdzad pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ chos yang dag par bsdu ba dang/ rtsis kyi ming bsdu ba'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa dang/ yi ge lnga dang yi ge drug
13b2(rgyud 'grel): gi stong pa chen po dang thig le stong pa la bstod pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa zhes bya ba ni ye shes kyi le'u la'o// //des na rim pa 'dis gsungs pa'i phyir le'u lnga'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa'i bcom ldan 'das dus kyi 'khor lo ni 'dir brjod par bya'o/ /'dir ston par
13b3(rgyud 'grel): byed pa'i le'u'i tshogs rgyud kyi rgyal po ni rjod par byed pa'o/ /brjod bya rjod byed 'di dag phan tshun brjod bya rjod byed kyis mtshan nyid ni 'brel ba ste/ brjod par bya ba ni bcom ldan 'das dus kyi 'khor lo le'u lnga'i ngo bo nyid kyis zhugs pa yin la/ rjod par byed pa ni dus ni 'khor lo rjod par byed pa
13b4(rgyud 'grel): le'u lnga'i bdag nyid do/ /yang dang po'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das ni brjod par bya ba yin la/ rjod par byed pa ni dang po'i sangs rgyas rjod par byed pa'o/ /zhes bya ba brjod bya rjod byed kyi mtshan nyid ni brjod bya rjod byed kyi 'brel ba'o/ /de nas dkyil 'khor du zhugs pa las 'jig rten pa'i dbang
13b5(rgyud 'grel): sbyin pas bsod nams kyi tshogs kyi don byed pa ni dgos pa'o/ /shes rab chen po 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dbang bzhi pa sbyin pas rigs med pa phyag rgya chen po'i dngos grub thob pa la/ bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs kyi don byed pa ni dgos pa'i dgos pa ste/ brjod bya la sogs pa'i mtshan
13b6(rgyud 'grel): nyid 'di dag nyid mngon par gzigs nas/ gdul bya'i skye bo des pa dang bral ba rnams la rang gi sems kyi bsam pas shes bya ba la/ nges pa ni nyan thos pa'i mchog gi sdom pa 'dod pa lnga la nye bar longs spyod pa dang bral ba'i tshul khrims kyi sdom pa ste de dang bral ba ni nges
13b7(rgyud 'grel): pa dang bral ba'o/ /de dag gi rang gi sems kyi bsam pa ni 'dod pa lnga la nye bar longs spyod par 'dod pa'o/ /de bzhin du dbang po gnyis kyis bde ba chen po 'dod pa ni nges pa dang bral ba rnams kyi rang gi sems kyi bsam pa ste/ rang gi sems kyi bsam pa 'dis skye ba 'di la sangs rgyas nyid
14a1(rgyud 'grel): kyi/ 'bras bu rab tu ster ba zhes bya ba ni skye ba 'di'i mi'i skye ba la sangs rgyas nyid kyi 'bras bu rab tu ster ba rgyud kyi rgyal po'o/ /lha la sogs pa 'gro ba lnga'i skye ba la ni ma yin no/ /de ci'i phyir zhe na/ las kyi ma yin par skyes pa'i phyir ro/ /
14a2(rgyud 'grel): 'dir lha la sogs pa rnams la yang mi'i skye ba thob nas sangs rgyas nyid kyi 'bras bu rab tu gter bar 'gyur ro zhes bya ba ni bcom ldan 'das kyis nges pa'o/ /bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs dag dang khams drug gi bdag nyid can skyes bu chen po'i
14a3(rgyud 'grel): gang zag la'o/ /zhes pa ste/ rnam pa gzhan du las ngan pa dang ldan pa'i mi'i skye ba 'di la sangs rgyas nyid kyi 'bras bu rab tu ster ba ni ma yin no/ /zhes bya ba de bzhin gshegs pa'i nges pa'o/ /cis te sngags kyi theg pa 'dir sangs rgyas bcom ldan
14a4(rgyud 'grel): 'das kyis gsungs pa ni 'di lta ste/ gdol ba smyig ma mkhan sogs dang/ /mtshams med lnga rnams ni byed pa rnams/ /sngags kyi spyod pa rjes spyad na/ /skye 'di nyid la sangs rgyas 'gyur/ zhes pa yin no zhe na/ bcom ldan 'das kyi gsung 'di ni bden
14a5(rgyud 'grel): te/ skye ba 'di la sngar mtshams med pa lnga la sogs pa mi gzad pa'i las gang byas pa de dag sngags kyi theg pa 'dir phyag rgya chen po mi 'gyur ba'i bde ba'i ting nge 'dzin gyis bcom nas/ mi dge ba glo bur ba bzhan mi 'jug par bya ba'i phyir/ /rdo rje
14a6(rgyud 'grel): chos 'byung gi khang par bdud bzhi dang bgegs kyi dgra 'jug pa'i sgo rnams la/ byams pa dang snying rje dang dga' ba dang/ btang snyoms la sogs pa dang byang chub kyi phyogs kyi sgo glegs bcug nas/ /de nyid du rdo rje sems dpa' dang phyag rgya chen
14a7(rgyud 'grel): po dang/ lhan cig tu bsgrubs te mtshams med pa lnga byed pa po rnams kyang skye ba 'di la sangs rgyas nyid kyi 'bras bu thob par 'gyur ro zhes pa ni de bzhin gshegs pa bzhed kyi/ sngags kyi theg par zhugs pa'i rjes la mtshams med pa lnga la
14b1(rgyud 'grel): sogs pa mi bzad pa'i las byed pa rnams kyang skye ba 'di la sangs rgyas nyid kyi 'bras bu thob par 'gyur ro zhes bya ba ni de bzhin gshegs pa yang dag par bzhed pa ma yin no/ /'dir theg pa gsum ga la yang bcom ldan 'das kyi gsung ni thog mar dge ba/ bar
14b2(rgyud 'grel): du dge ba/ tha mar dge ba zhes bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa'i phyir/ sngags kyi theg pa la zhugs pa'i rjes la sdig pa byas dang sangs rgyas nyid kyi 'bras bu thob par 'gyur ro zhes pa ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i nges pa ma yin no/ /'o na sngags kyi theg pa 'dir
14b3(rgyud 'grel): rnal 'byor pa rnams kyis sha bza' bar bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs la/ de nyid kyang rtag tu srog bcad pa las 'byung ste/ srog gcad pa med par ni 'ga' zhig gi tshe srid do/ /gal te za ba po med na gsod pa po yang mi 'byung ngo/ /de'i phyir za ba po dang gsod
14b4(rgyud 'grel): pa po dag srog gcod par 'gyur ro/ /'dir yang nyi ma so sor sngags pas dam tshig bzhi bya'o/ zhes pa ni de bzhin gshegs pas nges pa'o zhe na/ de ni bden te/ rgyu gang gi phyir mtshan ma dang kha na ma tho ba dang bcas pas srog gcod par 'gyur ba/ rgyu de'i phyir
14b5(rgyud 'grel): rnal 'byor ba rnams kyi mtshan ma med pa dang kha na ma tho ba med pa go ku la sogs pa bza' bar bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs so/ /'dir yul gang na 'jig rten pa rnams kyis gang bza' ba ma yin pa dang/ gang gtsod ba ma yin pa go ku la sogs
14b6(rgyud 'grel): pa rang gi las kyis shi ba dang/ g.yul du las ngan pa 'am rang gi skyon gyi chom rkun la sogs pas gsang ba de dag thams cad rnal 'byor bas bza' bar de bzhin gshegs pas gsungs so/ /rdzas kyis nyos pa ni ma yin zhing pa med la sogs pa dang
14b7(rgyud 'grel): mchod sbyin la sogs pa'i bya ba la gsang ba yang ma yin te/ mtshan ma dang bcas pa'i sha bza' o zhes ni de bzhin gshegs pas ma gsungs so/ /yang gang zhig nyi ma so sor dam tshig bya ba de ni kha na ma tho ba med pa'i go ku la sogs pa lnga
15a1(rgyud 'grel): lnga dang/ rnam par snang mdzad la sogs pa lnga'i ri lu yungs kar kyi tshad tsam nyi ma so sor dam tshig bsten pa'i don du bya'o/ /rtag par kha na ma tho ba med pa'i chang dang bud med ni bsgom pa'i slad du rmongs pa med pa'i chos kyis gsungs
15a2(rgyud 'grel): so/ /rtsa ba'i rgyud las kyang bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa 'di lta ste/ lha dang rang 'jigs pha mes dang/ /'dod grub don dang btsong phyir yang/ /gdul ka sdig pa byed rnams kyis/ /gnod byed min pa'i sems can bsad/ /de yi sha de nyo ba dang//
15a3(rgyud 'grel): za 'dod kha na ma tho bcas/ /ma blangs snod du lhung gyur pa/ /de nyid kha na ma tho med/ /srog chags cig gi sha dag ni/ /mang po rnams kyis thos pa mchog /srog chags du ma'i sha dag ni/ /yid skyes gcig gis zos pa min/ /snying rje skyed de de
15a4(rgyud 'grel): nyid las/ /rnam par mi rtog sems kyis ni/ /rnal 'byor ldan pas bza' bya ba/ /kha na ma tho med gzhan min/ /rigs su 'dzin pa gzhom pa'i phyir/ /rtag tu bza' dang btung ba dang/ /rigs min mngon bgrod rdo rje can/ /de nyid gzigs pa dag
15a5(rgyud 'grel): gis gsungs/ zhes pa'o/ /de ltar gsungs pa'i rim pas nges pa dang bral ba rnams la sangs rgyas nyid kyi 'bras bu rab tu ster ba ni rgyud kyi rgyal po'o/ /sangs rgyas nyid ni thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang/
15a6(rgyud 'grel): lam gyi rnam pa mkhyen pa nyid dang/ stobs bcu dang mi 'jigs pa la sogs pa'i yon tan rnam par 'byor pa ste/ de ster ba ni sangs rgyas nyid kyi 'bras bu rab tu ster ba'o/ /bde ba chen po'i gnas zhes pa ni/ bde ba chen po'i gnas
15a7(rgyud 'grel): chos kyi dbyings nam mkha' i mtshan nyid can/ dog ba med pa'i chos 'byung 'jig rten gyi dpe las 'das pa kun tu bzang po bde ba chen po bde ba chen po'i gnas so/ /mchog gi dang po'i sangs rgyas rdo rje dbyings gyi dkyil 'khor chen por
15b1(rgyud 'grel): zhes pa ni/ rigs med pa shes pa dang shes bya gcig tu 'dres par gyur cing/ gcad du med la dbyer med pa/ rnam pa thams cad du dbyings kyi mtshan nyid me long gi pra phab pa dang mtshungs pa ste/ rdo rje dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor chen po der ro/ /
15b2(rgyud 'grel): rdo rje seng ge'i khri la bzhugs pa ni/ rdo rje seng ge'i khri zla ba dang/ nyi ma dang me'i dkyil bcad du med cing dbyer med pa 'am/ e'i yi ge nam mkha' i khams ni rdo rje seng ge'i khri'o/ /de la bzhugs pa ni rdo rje seng ge'i khri la bzhugs pa sku dang gsung
15b3(rgyud 'grel): dang thugs dang ye shes kyi bdag nyid waM yig ste/ rdo rje seng ge'i khri la bzhugs pa de yis so/ /sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' dang khro bo'i rgyal po dang lha dang klu dang lha dang lha mo'i tshogs kyis yongs su bskor ba zhes pa/ sangs rgyas
15b4(rgyud 'grel): ni mi bskyod pa la sogs pa'o/ /byang chub sems dpa' ni kun tu bzang po la sogs pa'o/ /khro bo'i rgyal po ni gtsug tor la sogs pa'o/ /lha ni dbang phyug la sogs pa'o/ /klu ni mdza' yas la sogs pa'o/ /lha mo ni rdo rje dbyings ni dbang phyug
15b5(rgyud 'grel): ma la sogs pa dang/ chos kyi dbyings ma la sogs pa dang/ shin tu sngon mo la sogs pa dang/ tsar tsI ka la sogs pa dang/ gau rI la sogs pa dang/ khyi gdod ma la sogs pa ste/ de dag gi 'dus pa ni tshogs so/ /de yis yongs su
15b6(rgyud 'grel): bskor ba ni/ lha dang lha mo'i tshogs kyis yongs su bskor ba ste/ lha dang lha mo'i tshogs kyis yongs su bskor ba yis so/ /khams gsum pas zhabs kyi pad+ma la phyag byas pa zhes pa la/ khams gsum pa ni 'dod pa dang gzugs dang gzugs med
15b7(rgyud 'grel): pa ste/ de dag gi gang gi zhabs kyi pad+ma la phyag byas pa de ni khams gsum pas zhabs kyi pad+ma la phyag byas pa ste/ khams gsum pas zhabs kyi pad+ma la phyag byas pa de yis so/ /khams gsum pa'i 'khor los sgyur ba zhes pa ni/ gang gi
16a1(rgyud 'grel): chos kyi 'khor lo khams gsum du gcig car rab tu 'khor ba de ni khams gsum pa'i 'khor los sgyur ba ste/ khams gsum pa'i 'khor los sgyur ba de yis so/ /mchog gi dang po'i sangs rgyas zhes pa la/ mchog gi
16a2(rgyud 'grel): dang po'i sangs rgyas ni skad cig gcig dang rnam pa lnga dang rnam pa nyi shu dang sgyu 'phrul dra bas mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa'i mtshan nyid 'gyur ba med pa'i bde ba ni mchog yin la/ de yis dang por sangs rgyas pa ni mchog gi dang po'i sangs
16a3(rgyud 'grel): rgyas te/ mchog gi dang po'i sangs rgyas de yis so/ /rigs med pa zhes pa la/ rigs ni shes rab dang thabs kyis bdag nyid gzung ba dang 'dzin pa'i mtshan nyid kyis chos te/ rigs de gang gis spangs pa de ni rigs med pa ste/ rigs med
16a4(rgyud 'grel): pa de yis so/ /bcom ldan 'das dus kyi 'khor lo zhes pa la/ bcom ldan ni bdud dang nyon mongs pa bcom pa'i phyir bcom pa dang/ dbang phyug la sogs pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i yon tan gyi tshogs te/ bcom pa de 'di la ldan pa'i phyir
16a5(rgyud 'grel): bcom ldan no/ /dus ni mchog tu mi 'gyur ba'i bde ba chen po'i mtshan nyid de/ de yis gang gi lus phung po dang khams la sogs pa sgrib pa med pa'i 'khor lor bskyed pa de ni dus kyi 'khor lo'o/ /gzhan yang yi ge so so re re ste/ kA
16a6(rgyud 'grel): yig gis ni rgyu zhi ba/ /la yig 'di la thim pa nyid/ /tsa yig gis ni g.yo ba'i sems/ /kra yig rim pa bcings las so/ /rim pa ni lus la sogs pa'i thig le rnams 'pho ba yin la/ de lhan cig skyes pa'i bde bas bcings pa
16a7(rgyud 'grel): ni kA la tsakra ste/ bcom ldan 'das dus kyi 'khor lo de yis so/ /zla ba bzang pos gsol ba btab par gyur pa yis zhes pa ni/ 'di ni zla ba yang yin la bzang po yang yin pa'i phyir zla ba bzang po ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
16b1(rgyud 'grel): kyi nyan pa por gyur ba rdo rje zla ba dri ma med pa'i 'od do/ /sems can thams cad kyi skad tha dad pa gang gis de bzhin gshegs pas chos gsungs pa rnams yang dag par sdud par byed pa'i phyir de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi nyan pa por gyur pa'i gsang ba'i
16b2(rgyud 'grel): bdag po ste/ gsang ba ni nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa dag las mchog tu gyur pa rdo rje'i theg pa'o/ /de'i yang dag par sdud pa po yin pas na bdag po ste/ gsang ba'i bdag po'o/ /de bzhin du phyi rol du ni 'jig rten gyi bden pas gsang ba'i
16b3(rgyud 'grel): sgra gnod sbyin rnams te/ de dag gi bdag po ni gsang ba'i bdag po'o/ /ro ldan na gnas pa ni phyi rol du ro'i sgras srog nyams pa shi ba'i tshogs so/ /de 'di la yod pa'i phyir ro/ /ldan te dur khrod kyi sa'o/ /de nas gnod sbyin chen po sems can
16b4(rgyud 'grel): rnams la rnam par tho 'tsham zhing bgegs du ma byed pa po dag yod la/ de dag gsod par byed pa po ni ro ldan na gnas pa ste/ nags kyi ri dags kyi bdag po zhes pa bzhin du ro ldan na gnas pa gnod sbyin chen po rnams kyi bdag po'o/ /nang du ni ro zhes
16b5(rgyud 'grel): pa/ dbugs 'byung ba dang 'jug pa sum stong drug brgyas dman pa'i nyi khri chig stong drug brgya rnams 'gog pa'o/ /de 'di la yod pa ni chos kyi sprin gyi sa ste/ de la gnas pa ni ro ldan na gnas pa'o/ /bdud dang nyon mongs pa dang shes bya dang snyoms 'jug gi
16b6(rgyud 'grel): sgrib pa'i gnod sbyin rnams gsod par byed pa ni gnod sbyin gyi bdag po ste/ de bzhin gshegs pas chos kyi seng+ge'i sgra dang sems can so so'i sgra dag gis bstan pa'i chos rnams rab tu ston par byed pa po sprul pa'i sku phyag na rdo rje zla ba bzang pos gsol ba btab
16b7(rgyud 'grel): par gyur pa de yis so/ /mchog gi dang po'i sangs rgyas shes pa ni/ brjod bya mchog gi dang po'i sangs rgyas rjod par byed pa'i phyir te/ brjod bya 'di rjod par byed pa'i ngo bo nyid kyis gnas pa'i phyir mchog gi dang po'i sangs rgyas so/ /dus kyi 'khor ni brjod bya dus
17a1(rgyud 'grel): kyi 'khor lo brjod par byed pa'i phyir dus kyi 'khor lo'i rjod par byed do/ /stong phrag bcu gnyis pa zhes pa ni/ stong phrag brgyad cu rtsa bzhi lhag pa'i 'bum phrag gsum gyi yi ge'i tshogs te/ yi ge sum cu rtsa gnyis pa rjes su bsngags pa stong
17a2(rgyud 'grel): phrag bcu gnyis yod pa ni stong phrag bcu gnyis pa'o/ /rigs med pa zhes pa ni/ brjod bya rigs med pa brjod par byed pa'i phyir ro/ /'dir rigs ni shes rab kyi phyogs dang thabs kyi phyogs te/ phyogs spangs pa gang gi phyir rigs de med pa'i rgyud de ni rigs med
17a3(rgyud 'grel): pa shes rab dang/ thabs kyi bdag nyid can rnal 'byor gyi rgyud ces rgyal bas gnyis su med par gsungs so/ /brjod par bya ba thabs dang shes rab kyi bdag nyid can gyi rgyud kyi rgyal po 'di la thabs dang shes rab kyi phyogs tha dad na/ thabs dang shes rab kyi bdag nyid
17a4(rgyud 'grel): can gyi brjod par bya ba med par 'gyur ro/ /thabs dang shes rab kyi bdag nyid can gyi brjod par bya ba med na/ gnyis su med pa'i ye shes med par 'gyur ro/ /gnyis su med pa'i ye shes med na sangs rgyas nyid kyang med par 'gyur ro/ /sangs rgyas nyid med na 'khor
17a5(rgyud 'grel): ba pa'o/ /'dir rjod par byed pa dang brjod par bya ba'i 'brel pa med par thabs kyi ming can rnal 'byor gyi rgyud la thabs dang shes rab kyi bdag nyid gnyis su med pa dang rnal 'byor brjod bya rjod byed kyi mtshan nyid du mi 'gyur ro/ /rnal 'byor gyi sgra ni thabs kyi
17a6(rgyud 'grel): don rjod par byed pa 'am/ shes rab kyi don rjod par byed pa yang ma yin te/ rnal 'byor gyi sgra ni thabs dang shes rab kyi don rjod par byed pa'o/ /de bzhin du yang gsungs pa/ rnal 'byor thabs kyi lus dang ni/ /shes rab gcig pu dag gi min/ /
17a7(rgyud 'grel): thabs dang shes rab snyoms 'jug pa/ /de bzhin gshegs pas rnal 'byor gsungs zhes so/ /de'i phyir rgyud gang la thabs dang shes rab kyi bdag nyid kyi brjod par bya ba yang pa'i rgyud de ni don dam par shes rab kyi rgyud kyang ma yin la/ thabs kyi
17b1(rgyud 'grel): rgyud kyang ma yin no/ /'jig rten gyi kun rdzob tu me long lta bu'i ye shes la sogs pa'i dbye bas phung po dang khams rnam par dag pa las thabs dang shes rab kyi phyogs su dbang po brtul pa'i sems can gyi bsam pa'i dbang gis de bzhin gshegs pas gsungs so/ /de bzhin
17b2(rgyud 'grel): du rnal 'byor ma'i ming can la yang ngo/ /'dir 'di la rnal 'byor gyi dang tshul yod pa'i phyir rnal 'byor pa'o/ /de bzhin du rnal 'byor ma yang ngo/ /de'i phyir gzhan la bltos pa nyid las rnal 'byor gyi rgyud dang rnal 'byor ma'i rgyud du yang 'gyur ro/ /des na don dam pa'i bden pas thabs
17b3(rgyud 'grel): dang shes rab kyi bdag nyid can rnal 'byor gyi rgyud rigs med pa dus kyi 'khor lo'o/ /rdo rje 'dzin pa'i ye shes kyi sku mngon du gyur pa'i mtshan yang dag par brjod pas 'khyud pa zhes pa ni dang po'i sangs rgyas mngon par brjod pa nyid kyi phyir ro/ /'dir ji ltar mtshan yang dag par
17b4(rgyud 'grel): brjod pa 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyis gsungs pa dang gsung bar 'gyur ba dang/ gsungs pa de bzhin du dang po'i sangs rgyas kyang ngo/ /dang po'i sgras ni thog ma dang tha ma med pa'i don to/ /thog ma med pa'i dus su thog ma
17b5(rgyud 'grel): med pa'i sangs rgyas kyis bstan pa dang ston par 'gyur ba dang/ ston pa ste de bzhin gshegs pa mar me mdzad dang/ shAkya thub pa 'ba' zhig gis gsungs pa ni ma yin no/ /'dir phyag na rdo rjes/ 'das pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyis gsungs/ /ma 'ongs rnams kyang gsung
17b6(rgyud 'grel): 'gyur la/ /da ltar byung ba rdzogs sangs rgyas/ /yang yang gsungs pa gang yin dang/ /rgyud chen sgyu 'phrul dra ba 'dir/ /rdo rje 'chang chen gsang sngags 'chang/ /dpag med dgyes pa rnam dag gis/ /gang yang yang dag glur blangs pa/ zhes gsungs so/ /mtshan yang dag par
17b7(rgyud 'grel): brjod pa gsol ba 'debs pa'i tshig 'di'i phyir de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis sngags kyi theg pa gsungs pa yin no/ /'dir 'dus pa las/ de bzhin gshegs pa mar me mdzad nas shAkya thub pa'i bar du de bzhin gshegs pa gang gis kyang sngags kyi theg pa
18a1(rgyud 'grel): ma gsungs so/ zhes pa gang yin pa de ni/ de'i tshe de'i dus na zhes pa ste/ 'phags pa'i yul du chos ston pa'i dus na/ rigs bzhi'i mngon pa'i nga rgyal dang ldan zhing skal ba med pa'i sems can rnams kyi bsam pa'i dbang gis 'phags pa'i
18a2(rgyud 'grel): yul du 'khor rnams la ma bstan te/ dus gzhan du yul gzhan gyi 'jig rten gyi khams kyi 'khor la yang ma bstan pa ni ma yin no/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung 'di'i phyir/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad theg pa gsum ston par byed pa po yin no/ /rnam pa
18a3(rgyud 'grel): gzhan du na thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du mi 'gyur te/ /rdo rje'i theg pa ston par byed pa po nyid ma yin pa'i phyir ro/ /de'i phyir sems can gyi bsam pa'i dbang gis/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad theg pa gsum ston par byed pa po dang/ chos kyi phung po brgyad khri bzhi stong
18a4(rgyud 'grel): ston par byed pa po yin no/ /de'i phyir rdo rje 'dzin pa'i ye shes kyi sku mngon du gyur pa'i mtshan yang dag par brjod pas 'khyud pa'o// //rgyud kyi rgyal po thams cad kyi rdo rje'i tshig mngon du gyur pa zhes pa ni/ rdo rje theg pa 'dir sems can gyi
18a5(rgyud 'grel): bsam pa'i dbang gis/ rgyud kyi rgyal po thams cad la rdo rje'i tshig tu sbas te/ bzhi pa de yang de bzhin no/ /zhes de bzhin gshegs pas gsungs pa'i phyir ro/ /bzhi pa ni gsum pa ma yin te bzhi pa zhes gsungs pa'i phyir ro de yang de bzhin no zhes gsungs pa'i
18a6(rgyud 'grel): phyir shes rab ye shes de nyid bzhi par 'gyur ro/ /bcom ldan 'das kyis gsung 'di'i phyir rdo rje'i tshig tu sbas pa yin no/ /rgyud kyis rgyal po thams cad la rdo rje'i tshig rab tu gsal ba ma yin zhing/ bla ma rgyud pa'i rim pas rtogs par bya ba yin to/ /rgyud ni/ rgyud gzhan
18a7(rgyud 'grel): dag gis rtogs par bya zhes de bzhin gshegs pas gsungs pa'i phyir ro/ /sngags kyi tshul 'di la rdo rje'i tshig rnam pa gnyis te/ gcig ni 'jig rten pa'i kun rdzob yin la gnyis pa ni don dam pa'o/ /de dag las 'jig rten kun rdzob gyi rdo rje'i tshig ni
18b1(rgyud 'grel): gsod pa la sogs pa'i las la dam tshig grub pa ster bar byed pa'o/ /don dam pa'i bden pa'i rdo rje'i tshig ni bzhi pa de yang de bzhin te phyag rgya chen po'i dngos grub kyi 'bras bu ster bar byed pa'o/ /dang po'i sangs rgyas 'di la rdo rje'i tshig de dag nyid rab tu gsal bar
18b2(rgyud 'grel): bstan pa dang bshad pa dang rab tu bshad pa bdag gis bcom ldan 'das kyis gsal bar mdzad do/ /'di nyid bsgrub pa la phyag rgya chen po bsgom pa du ba la sogs pa mtshan ma'i lam rab tu gsal bar mdzad de/ stong par rtse gcig yid byas te/ nyi ma gcig ni yongs su
18b3(rgyud 'grel): brtag ces pas so/ /bcom ldan 'das kyi gsung 'di'i phyir/ mchog gi dang po'i sangs rgyas la rdo rje'i tshig phyag rgya chen po bsgom pa'i lam du ba la sogs pa rab tu gsal ba yin gyi/ bla ma rgyud pa'i rim pas 'ongs pa ma yin la/ bla ma'i bka' yis byin gyis
18b4(rgyud 'grel): brlabs pa yang ma yin no/ /lam 'di la yang nyin dang mtshan mor yid ches pa yod de/ nyi ma cig ni yongs su brtag ces bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa'i phyir ro/ /'dir du ba la sogs pa'i mtshan ma bor nas gzhan sngags la sogs pa'i sgrub thabs
18b5(rgyud 'grel): nyi ma gcig gis rnal 'byor pas yongs su brtag par bya ba ma yin no/ /mtshan ma yang rnam pa gsum ste/ dang po'i mtshan ma dang/ bar ma'i mtshan ma dang/ tha ma'i mtshan ma'o/ /dang po'i mtshan ma ni du ba la sogs pa'i lam dang/ sbyor ba yan
18b6(rgyud 'grel): lag drug gi sku rdzogs pa'i 'gyur ba med pa skad cig thob pa'o/ /bar ma'i mtshan ma ni mchog tu mi 'gyur ba'i skad cig brgya phrag bco brgyad kyis sa dang po thob pa dang/ mngon par shes pa lnga dang/ ma mthong ba'i don yang dag par mthong ba dang/ 'jig rten
18b7(rgyud 'grel): pa'i dngos grub thob pa'o/ /tha ma'i mtshan ma ni sangs rgyas nyid dang/ rdo rje 'chang nyid de/ mchog tu mi 'gyur ba'i skad cig drug brgya lhag pa'i stong phrag nyi shu rtsa gcig gis sa bcu gnyis pa thob nas phyag rgya chen po'i dngos grub thob pa'o/ /rdo rje'i tshig la
19a1(rgyud 'grel): sogs pa mtshan ma sngon du 'gro ba can 'di dag rab tu gsal bar rgyud kyi rgyal po mchog gi dang po'i sangs rgyas las bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs so/ /de'i phyir rgyud ni rgyud gzhan tshol ba rnams la rgyud kyi rgyal po thams cad kyi rdo rje'i
19a2(rgyud 'grel): tshig mngon du gyur pa'o/ /sangs rgyas rin chen za ma tog kha 'byed pa zhes pa la/ sangs rgyas rin chen ni mchog tu mi 'gyur ba'i bde ba yin la/ za ma tog ni rdo rje dang pad+ma ste sangs rgyas rin chen za ma tog go /de nyid rgyud kyi rgyal po gang gis kha 'byed pa de ni
19a3(rgyud 'grel): sangs rgyas rin chen za ma tog kha 'byed pa'o/ /'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i bden pa la brten pa zhes pa la/ 'jig rten pa'i bden pa ni dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lo rnam par rtog pa bsgom pa bskyed pa'i rim pas 'jig rten pa'i dngos grub sgrub par
19a4(rgyud 'grel): byed pa'o/ /'jig rten las 'das pa'i bden pa ni du ba la sogs pa'i mtshan ma dang rnam par mi rtog pa'i sems rdzogs pa'i rim pas phyag rgya chen po'i dngos grub sgrub par byed pa'o/ /rdzogs pa'i rim pa ni lhan cig skyes pa rnam par mi rtog pa ste/ rnam
19a5(rgyud 'grel): pa thams cad du zhal dang phyag dang kha dog dang dbyibs kyi rtog pa dang bral ba'o/ /bden pa 'di dag la bden pa ni 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i bden pa la bsten pa ste lam gnyis ka ston pa'i phyir ro/ /mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa
19a6(rgyud 'grel): bzhi dang rdo rje bzhis yongs su dag pa zhes pa ni skad cig gcig gis mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa dang/ rnam pa lngas mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa dang/ rnam pa nyi shus mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa dang/ sgyu 'phrul dra bas mngon
19a7(rgyud 'grel): par rdzogs par byang chub pa ste/ 'di rnams kyis yongs su dag pa ni mngal skyes skyed pa'i rim pa dang du ba la sogs pa sku rdzogs pa'i rim pas so/ /de ltar mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa bzhis yongs su dag pa'o/ /sku bzhi dang/ rigs drug dang/ bden
19b1(rgyud 'grel): pa bcu gnyis dang/ de kho na nyid bcu drug dang/ stong pa nyid bcu drug dang/ snying rje bcu drug dang/ 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dbang dang/ las dang ye shes dang phyag rgya chen mo'i dngos grub kyi lam rab tu gsal bar byed pa zhes pa la/ sku bzhi ni dag
19b2(rgyud 'grel): pa dang/ chos dang longs spyod rdzogs pa dang/ sprul pa rnams mngal skyes rnams kyi bzhi pa dang/ shin tu gnyid log pa dang/ rmi lam dang sad pa'i gnas skabs kyi mtshan nyid can te/ de dag kyang sangs rgyas rnams kyi sgrib pa dang bral ba'o/ /rigs drug ni mi 'gyur
19b3(rgyud 'grel): pa'i bde ba ye shes kyi khams dang/ rnam par shes pa nam mkha' i khams dang/ 'du byed rlung gi khams dang/ tshor ba me'i khams dang/ 'du shes chu'i khams dang/ gzugs sa'i khams te/ mngal skyes rnams kyi rigs drug sgrib pa dang bcas pa yin la/
19b4(rgyud 'grel): sangs rgyas rnams kyi sgrib pa dang bral ba'o/ /bden pa bcu gnyis ni/ ma rig pa dang/ 'du byed dang/ rnam par shes pa dang/ ming dang gzugs dang/ skye mched drug dang/ reg pa dang/ tshor ba dang/ sred pa dang/ len pa dang/ srid pa dang/ skye ba dang/ rga shi ste/ mngal
19b5(rgyud 'grel): skyes rnams kyi bden pa bcu gnyis ni sgrib pa dang bcas pa yin la/ sangs rgyas rnams kyi sgrib pa dang bral ba'o/ /'pho ba bcu gnyis kyi srog gi dbye bas srog gi rlung rgyu ba'i phyir mngal nas skyes pa rnams kyi sgrib pa dang bcas pa'o/ /yan lag bcu gnyis 'gags
19b6(rgyud 'grel): pa'i phyir sangs rgyas rnams kyi ni sgrib pa dang bral ba'o/ /de kho na nyid bcu drug ni/ sprul pa'i sku dang/ sprul pa'i gsung dang/ sprul pa'i thugs dang/ sprul pa'i ye shes dang/ longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku dang/ longs spyod rdzogs pa'i gsung dang/ longs spyod
19b7(rgyud 'grel): rdzogs pa'i thugs dang/ longs spyod rdzogs pa'i ye shes dang/ chos kyi sku dang/ chos kyi gsung dang/ chos kyi thugs dang/ chos kyi ye shes dang/ lhan cig skyes pa'i sku dang/ lhan cig skyes pa'i gsung dang/ lhan cig skyes pa'i thugs dang/ lhan cig
20a1(rgyud 'grel): skyes pa'i ye shes te/ dga' ba dang/ mchog dga' dang/ khyad par gyi dga' ba dang/ lhan cig skyes pa'i dbye bas de kho na nyid bcu drug mngal skyes rnams kyi ni sgrib pa dang bcas la yin te/ cu drug phyed phyed thig le 'dor ba'i phyir ro/ /sangs rgyas rnams
20a2(rgyud 'grel): kyi ni sgrib pa dang bral ba yin te/ bcu drug phyed phyed thig le 'dzin pa nyid kyi phyir ro/ /stong pa nyid bcu drug ces pa ni/ nag po'i phyogs dang nyi ma dang shes rab bo/ /snying rje bcu drug ces pa ni/ dkar po'i phyogs dang/ zla ba dang thabs so/ /stong pa nyid la dbye ba gsum
20a3(rgyud 'grel): ste stong pa nyid dang/ chen po stong pa nyid dang/ don dam pa stong pa nyid do/ /de la stong pa nyid ni phung po lnga stong pa nyid de nag po'i tshes gcig la sogs pa tshes lnga'o/ /chen po stong pa nyid ni khams lnga stong pa nyid de/ drug pa la sogs pa tshes lnga'o/ /don dam pa stong pa nyid ni
20a4(rgyud 'grel): dbang po lnga stong pa nyid de bcu gcig pa la sogs pa tshes lnga'o/ /des na gnam stong gi mthar thug pa tshes bco lnga ni stong pa nyid bco lnga'o/ /gnam stong gi mdza' dang dkar po'i tshes gcig gi dang po'i dbus su bcu drug pa rnam pa thams cad stong pa nyid do/ /de bzhin du snying rje rnam pa
20a5(rgyud 'grel): gsum ste/ sems can la dmigs pa dang/ chos la dmigs pa dang dmigs pa med pa'o/ /de la sems can la dmigs pa ni dkar po'i tshes gcig la sogs pa tshes lnga'o/ /chos la dmigs pa ni drug pa la sogs pa'i tshes lnga'o/ /dmigs pa med pa ni bcu gcig la
20a6(rgyud 'grel): sogs pa tshes lnga ste/ nya'i mthar thug pa'o/ /nya'i mdza' dang nag po'i tshes gcig 'jug pa'i dang po'i dbus su snying rje bcu dgu pa'o/ /'di dag gcig pa nyid ni stong pa nyid ni bcu drug dang/ snying rje bcu drug gi bdag nyid brjod par bya ba ste/ de'i rjod par byed pa'o/ /
20a7(rgyud 'grel): 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i mngon par dbang bskur ba zhes pa la/ re zhig 'jig rten pa ni/ chu dang cod pan dang/ dar dpyangs dang/ rdo rje dril bu dang/ brtul zhugs chen po dang/ ming dang/ rjes su gnang ba dang/ bum pa dang/ gsang ba dang/ shes rab ye
20b1(rgyud 'grel): shes te/ mngal nas skyes pa rnams kyis 'jig rten kun rdzob kyi dbang bcu ni lus dang ngag dang sems dang ye shes dang/ khams dang phung po dang/ skye mched dang las kyi dbang po la sogs pa yongs su dag par bya'o/ /'jig rten las 'das pa bcu gcig pa ni/ bzhi pa de yang de bzhin
20b2(rgyud 'grel): no zhes pa'i nges pas/ phyag rgya chen po mchog tu mi 'gyur ba'i ye shes kyi mtshan nyid bla ma'i zhal las lus dang ngag la sogs pa sgrib pa med pa nyid kyis sbyong bar byed pa'o/ /las dang ye shes dang phyag rgya chen po'i dngos grub ces pa la/ las kyi phyag rgya ni nu ma dang skar
20b3(rgyud 'grel): ldan pa'o/ /ye shes kyi phyag rgya ni rang gi sems kyis yongs su brtags pa'o/ /phyag rgya chen mo ni rnam par rtog pa dang bral ba pra phab pa'i rang bzhin can no/ /'di rnams kyi dngos grub ni rnam pa gsum ste/ 'dod pa na spyod pa ni las kyi phyag rgya'i dngos grub po/ /gzugs kyi srid pa'i dngos
20b4(rgyud 'grel): po'i mtshan nyid ni ye shes kyi phyag rgya'i dngos grub po/ /dngos po dang dngos po med pa dang bral ba rnams kun gyi mchog dang ldan pa ni phyag rgya chen mo'i dngos grub po/ /sku bzhi la sogs pa 'di dag gi 'jig rten dang 'ji rten las 'das pa'i lam rab tu gsal bar byed pa
20b5(rgyud 'grel): ni mchog gi dang po'i sangs rgyas so/ /de ltar brjod pa'i rim pas 'jig rten gyi khams dang/ nad dang/ dbang dang/ sgrub thabs dang/ ye shes te le'u lnga'i bdag nyid dam brtag pa lnga'i bdag nyid mi la sogs pa'i sems can mdza' dag gis yang dag par rdzogs pa'i
20b6(rgyud 'grel): sangs rgyas nyid thob pa'i phyir yang dag par bstan to/ /zhes pa ni yang dag pa'i rnam pa ste rdo rje'i tshig tu sbas pa'i rnam pas ni ma yin no/ /mchog gi dang po'i sangs rgyas 'di las bsdus pa'i rgyud yang dag par sdud par byed pa la 'jam dpal dang/ ma 'ongs pa'i dus
20b7(rgyud 'grel): su tshangs pa'i drang srong rnams gdul bar bya ba'i don du 'grel bshad byed pa la bdag dang/ rgyud ston par byed pa la gshin rje mthar byed la sogs pa rnams dang/ sham+b+ha la'i yul la sogs pa grong khyer bye ba phrag dgu bcu rtsa drug na gnas pa'i sems can thams
21a1(rgyud 'grel): cad theg pa chen po'i lam thob pa la de bzhin gshegs pas lung bstan to/ /zhes pa ni mchog gi dang po'i sangs rgyas stong phrag bcu gnyis pa 'di las bsdus pa'i rgyud yang dag par sdud par byed pa la 'jam dpal de bzhin gshegs
21a2(rgyud 'grel): pas lung bstan to/ /ma 'ongs pa'i dus su grong khyer kA la par gnas pa'i tshangs pa'i drang srong bye ba phrag phyed dang bzhi rnams gdul bar bya ba'i don du bsdus pa'i rgyud kyi 'grel bshad byed pa la 'jig rten dbang phyug bdag kyang lung bstan la/ gzhan khro bo'i
21a3(rgyud 'grel): rgyal po dang/ byang chub sems dpa' nyi shu rtsa gsum po dag kyang ngo/ /grong khyer bye ba phrag dgu cu rtsa drug na gnas pa'i sems can thams cad sprul pa'i sku bsdus pa'i rgyud ston par byed pa pos theg pa chen po'i lam thob par byed pa lung bstan to/ /theg pa chen
21a4(rgyud 'grel): po'i lam ni 'jam dpal gyi rdo rje'i rigs kyi bum pa dang/ gsang ba dang/ shes rab ye shes kyi dbang bskur ba ste/ de thob par byed pa la ni theg pa chen po'i lam thob par byed pa la'o/ /bum pa dang gsang ba dang/ ye shes kyi dbang bskur ba 'di las rigs thams cad
21a5(rgyud 'grel): rigs gcig tu 'gyur ro/ /rigs de 'di la yod pa'i phyir rigs ldan no/ /de'i rigs ni rigs ldan gyi rigs te/ sngags pa mdza' dag rdo rje'i rigs kyi dbang bskur ba'i phyir ro/ /zhes bya ba nges pa'i don to/ /de ltar 'jam dpal grags pa ni/ rigs ldan du 
21a6(rgyud 'grel): lung bstan cing// grags pa 'di'i rigs la 'jig rten dbang phyug bdag rigs ldan gnyis par lung bstan to/ /de bzhin du rim pa ji lta ba gshin rje mthar byed la sogs pa'i khro bo bcu dang/ sa'i snying po la sogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' bcu
21a7(rgyud 'grel): gsum po rnams te gshin rje mthar byed la sogs pa khro bo'i rgyal po de dag gi bar bar du byang chub sems dpa' bcu gsum po rnams lung bstan pa/ sprul pa'i sku yi grong khyer bye ba phrag dgu bcu rtsa drug na gnas pa rnams kyi rgyal por gyur pa/ sems
21b1(rgyud 'grel): can mdza' dag la de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos rab tu ston par mdzad pa/ kla klo la sogs pa'i chos ngan pa 'joms par mdzad pa/ skyes bu chen po'i mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis dang dpe byad brgyad cu dang ldan pa mngon par shes pa lnga la sogs pa dbang phyug gi yon tan
21b2(rgyud 'grel): yongs su rdzogs pa'o/ /de'i phyir mchog gi dang po'i sangs rgyas 'di las bsdus pa'i rgyud yang dag par (sdud par) byed pa la 'jam dpal dang/ 'grel bshad byed pa la bdag dang/ chos ston pa la gshin rje mthar byed la sogs pa rnams lung bstan to/ /bsdus pa'i rgyud kyi
21b3(rgyud 'grel): rgyal po dus kyi 'khor lo'i 'grel bshad rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi rjes su 'jug pa stong phrag bcu gnyis pa dri ma med pa'i 'od las brjod bya dang rjod byed dang 'brel pa dang dgos pa dang dgos pa'i dgos pa mngon par gzigs nas bcom ldan 'das kyi brgyud bstan pa'i mdor bsdus
21b4(rgyud 'grel): te gnyis pa'o// //da ni 'dir ston pa po dang gsol ba 'debs pa po'i 'brel pa yang brjod par bya'o/ /gal te na snga ma dang phyi mar rgyud kyi 'grel bshad ma thos pa'i tshig 'byung bar 'gyur te/ rdo rje'i theg pa 'di la ro ldan na/ /gnas pa'i
21b5(rgyud 'grel): gnod sbyin gyi bdag po chen po byang chub sems dpa' chen po phyag na rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa la gsol ba 'debs pa dang yang dag par sdud par byed pa po ma yin nam/ ji ltar sham+b+ha la'i yul ka lA pa'i grong gi bdag po nyi ma'i 'od kyi lha mo rnam par rgyal
21b6(rgyud 'grel): ma'i mngal nas byung ba rgyal po zla ba bzang po gsol ba 'debs pa por 'gyur/ rgyud gzhan 'ga' zhig tu yang ma thos shing lung bstan pa med pa'i phyir phan tshun ston pa po dang gsol ba 'debs pa po 'grel pa 'gal lo zhe na/ de'i phyir brjod par bya ste/ 'dir
21b7(rgyud 'grel): sngags kyi theg pa la mngal nas byung ba de bzhin gshegs pa la gsol ba 'debs pa por mi 'gyur ro zhes gang 'ga' zhig gis brjod pa de ni ma yin te/ gang gi phyir bcom ldan das kyang mngal nas byung ba nyid yin pa'i phyir ro/ /sngags kyi theg pa 'di
22a1(rgyud 'grel): la gal te mngal nas byung ba de bzhin gshegs pa la gsol ba 'debs pa po dang/ sdud pa por mi 'gyur na/ de'i tshe shAkya'i rigs mi'i dbang po zas gtsang ma'i lha mo sgyu 'phrul chen mo'i lhums nas bltams pa shAkya thub pa thams
22a2(rgyud 'grel): cad mkhyen pa ston pa por mi 'gyur te/ mngal nas byung ba nyid yin pa'i phyir ro/ /yang 'ga' zhig gis smras pa/ des sngar bdud bcom pa byas shing byang chub bskyed de/ de nas thams cad mkhyen pa chos ston par byed pa por gyur to/ /mya ngan las 'das pa'i rjes
22a3(rgyud 'grel): la yang mngal du 'jug pa med do zhes pa'i tshig las ni/ shin tu 'gal ba ste/ /rang ma grub par gzhan gyi sgrub byed ma yin pa'i phyir ro/ /'dir dang por sangs rgyas nyid med na lha dang mi dang lha ma yin gyi nang nas gang gis kyang bdud 'joms par mi byed do/ /dang
22a4(rgyud 'grel): por mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas par yang mi byed de/ sgrib pa thams cad med pa yin pa'i phyir ro/ /cig car yang mi byed de/ gang gi tshe bdud yod pa de'i tshe sangs rgyas nyid ma yin te/ sems sgrib pa dang bcas pa'i phyir ro/ /gang gi tshe sangs rgyas nyid yin
22a5(rgyud 'grel): pa de'i tshe bdud med de sems sgrib pa dang bral ba'i phyir ro zhes pa las gzhan pa ci yod/ /las kyi sa 'dir sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das ma gtogs pa bud med kyi mngal nas skyes pa gzhan ni skyes bu chen po'i mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis dang/ dpe byad brgyad
22a6(rgyud 'grel): cu dang/ mdzod spu sum cu rtsa gnyis su yongs su 'khyil ba dang/ mngon par shes pa drug dang ldan pa ma yin no/ /de'i phyir bdud ces bya ba ni sems can rnams kyi 'khor ba'i sems kyi bag chags kyi dri ma'o/ /sangs rgyas nyid ces bya ba 'di 'khor ba'i
22a7(rgyud 'grel): bag chags dang bral ba'i sems so/ /de ltar yang bcom ldan 'das kyis shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa las/ sems gang zhig yod pa'i sems de ni sems ma yin no/ zhes pa rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal bar gsungs te/ de nyid ni 'khor ba'i
22b1(rgyud 'grel): bag chags dang bral ba'o/ /de'i phyir bdud ni dri ma dang bcas pa'i sems yin la/ sangs rgyas nyid ni dri ma med pa'i sems yin no/ /'dir phyi rol tu sangs rgyas kyis bdud bcom pa gang yin pa de ni rmi lam bzhin du sems can rnams kyi rang gi sems kyi snang
22b2(rgyud 'grel): pa yin no/ /don dam par de bzhin gshegs pa'i thugs ni le'u lnga par rgyas par brjod par bya'o/ /'dir sems can gyi don du sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams 'khor bar 'jug pa ni 'khor ba pa rnams kyi brjod par bya ba ma yin no/ /'jig rten
22b3(rgyud 'grel): dbang phyug bdag sems can gyi don la dmyal bar zhugs pa'i dus su gshin rje'i pho nya rnams dang/ gshin rje'i rgyal pos bstod pa brjod pa/ gang zhig srid pa'i 'ching ba rnams las grol yang sems can don du srid pa 'dzin/ /de ni stong pa'i don dag ston
22b4(rgyud 'grel): mdzad dus las las kyi 'bras bu gtong ma yin/ /sems kyi dri ma yang dag ye shes mes bsregs rtag tu yang dag brtse bas brlan/ /mdzad spyod brtag min sems can don la dge ba'i sangs rgyas de la bdag cag 'dud/ ces pa'o/ /de'i phyir
22b5(rgyud 'grel): sems can gyi don gyi dor sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams mngal du 'jug pa 'am dmyal bar gshegs pa ni byis pa'i skye bo rnams kyis rnam par brtag par mi nus so/ /pha rol tu phyin pa bcu sgrubs pa sa bcu'i dbang phyug dbang bcu thob
22b6(rgyud 'grel): pa'i byang chub sems dpa' gcig gis kyang stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams su sprul pa'i sku du ma dag gis byang chub sems dpa' i gdul bya rnams la byang chub sems dpa' i chos ston par byed de/ byang chub sems dpa' chen po de du ma
22b7(rgyud 'grel): ni ma yin no/ /de bzhin du sngon gyi smon lam gyi stobs kyis bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs yongs su rdzogs shing/ mi 'jigs pa la sogs pa'i dbang phyug gi yon tan thams cad phun sum tshogs pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das ni sangs
23a1(rgyud 'grel): rgyas kyi zhing stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams rnams su sgyu ma'i sprul pa'i sku sgrib pa dang bral ba mdza' yas pa mdza' yas pa dag gis sems can mdza' yas pa mdza' yas pa dag gis skad mdza' yas pa dang/ /
23a2(rgyud 'grel): mdza' yas pa dag gi gsol ba 'debs pa po sna tshogs kyis gsol ba btab pa na/ sems can thams cad kyi skad la rab tu 'jug pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i skad kyis 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos ston par mdzad de/ thams cad mkhyen
23a3(rgyud 'grel): pa de du ma ni ma yin no/ /dper na sgyu ma'i skyes bu chen po 'ga' zhig gis sgyu ma'i gzugs du ma sprul te/ de'i sprul pa'i gzugs de dag gis shing rnams rtsa ba nas 'byin par byed cing/ ri'i rtse mo yang skyod par byed pa la/ lha chen po'i gzugs lta bu dang
23a4(rgyud 'grel): khyab 'jug lta bus lha byin la sogs pa 'ching bar byed de/ sgyu ma'i skyes bu chen po de du ma ni ma yin no/ /de bzhin du sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sgyu ma'i sprul pa'i sku dag gis srid pa gsum du sems can gyi don mdzad pa'o/ /des na
23a5(rgyud 'grel): sems can thams cad la 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos bstan pa'i phyir sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das sngar sa bcu gnyis kyi dbang phyug tu gyur pa/ mkhas pa sgyu 'phrul chen po 'chang ba sgyu 'phrul chen po'i mig 'phrul dang ldan pa/ 'phags
23a6(rgyud 'grel): pa'i yul lum bi ni shAkya'i rigs mi'i dbang po zas gtsang ma'i lha mo sgyu 'phrul chen mo'i lhums nas bltams pa ni gzhon nu don grub yin la/ sa bcu'i dbang phyug phyag na rdo rje yang sham b+ha la'i yul ka lA pa'i grong du nyi ma'i 'od kyi lha mo rnam par rgyal
23a7(rgyud 'grel): ma'i mngal nas 'khrungs pa zla ba bzang po'o/ /sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das ni sangs rgyas kyi zhing du 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos bstan pa'i don du sa bcu gnyis mngon sum du mdzad nas shAkya thub par gyur to/ /byang chub sems dpa' phyag na
23b1(rgyud 'grel): rdo rje ni chu bo shI ta'i byang phyogs grong bye ba phrag dgu bcu rtsa drug na gnas pa'i gdul bya rnams rgyud kyi rgyal po mchog gi dang po'i sangs rgyas kyis yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi lam thob par bya ba'i phyir rgyal po zla ba bzang po gyur to/ /sangs rgyas dang byang chub
23b2(rgyud 'grel): sems dpa' 'di gnyis sprul pa'i sku 'am longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku dag gis ston pa po dang gsol ba 'debs pa por 'brel pa yin te/ snga ma dang phyi ma 'gal ba med pa'i phyir ro/ /phyag na rdo rje'i sprul pa'i sku rgyal po zla ba bzang po des sems can thams cad kyis
23b3(rgyud 'grel): 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dngos grub bsgrub pa'i don du de bzhin gshegs pa la gsol ba btab po/ /de bzhin gshegs pas kyang chu bo shI ta'i byang phyogs sham+b+ha la la sogs pa'i yul rnams kyi grong khyer bye ba phrag dgu bcu rtsa drug na gnas pa rnams
23b4(rgyud 'grel): kyi sems rnam par dag ba/ skal ba dang ldan pa nyid du gnas pa gzigs nas rdo rje'i tshig kha ma phye ba med pa rdo rje'i tshig rab tu gsal bar byed pa mchog gi dang po'i sangs rgyas stong phrag bcu gnyis pa yang dag par bstan to/ /ma 'ongs pa'i dus su tshangs pa'i drang srong bye
23b5(rgyud 'grel): ba phrag phye dang bzhi dang grong bye ba phrag dgu bcu rtsa drug na gnas pa rnams yongs su smin par gzigs nas rgyud kyi rgyal po stong phrag bcu gnyis pa 'di las bsdus pa'i rgyud byed pa dang/ rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po ston par byed pa dang/ rdo rje'i rigs kyi dbang bcu rabs
23b6(rgyud 'grel): rigs thams cad rigs gcig tu byed pa la 'jam dpal grags pa rigs ldan du de bzhin gshegs pas lung bstan to/ /'grel bshad byed pa po pad+ma dkar po dag kyang rigs ldan gnyis par lung bstan to/ /de'i 'og tu bdag gi phyi nas gshin rje mthar byed la
23b7(rgyud 'grel): sogs pa rnams lung bstan to/ /'dir bcom ldan 'das kyis/ lo 'di nas ni drug brgya'i los/ /drang srong rnams ni smin don du/ /'jam dbyangs mi bdag grags pa ni/ /sham b+ha la zhes bya bar 'byung/ /'di yi sgrol ma lha mo che/ /sras ni pad 'dzin 'jig rten dbang
24a1(rgyud 'grel): bdag gi shAkya'i rigs rgyud las/ /byung ba zla bzangs khyod rigs la'o/ /smra mkhas rdo rje'i rigs dang ldan/ /grags pas rdo rje'i rigs la ni/ /rigs bzhi rigs gcig byas gang de/ /rigs ldan tshangs pa'i rigs kyi min/ /'di skad bdag gis thos
